The Yangtze River Water Level Has Gradually Stabilized 37

Rescue Efforts Underway for Breached Dikes in Anhui, Hubei, and Jiangxi

(Nanjing) The Yangtze River water level in the upper reaches has gradually stabilized, and today, the 13th, all regions experienced clear skies. The water level in Wanxian has receded another eight feet, indicating a promising trend. The Yangtze River Waterway Improvement Commission released the water level readings for various locations on the 13th:

(1) Upper reaches: Chongqing 49.6 feet, 0.2 feet higher than the 12th; Wanxian 92.9 feet, 8.0 feet lower than the 12th; Yichang 40.4 feet, 0.9 feet lower than the 12th; Shashi 31.7 feet, 0.2 feet lower than the 12th.

(2) Middle reaches: Yuezhou 47.1 feet, 0.8 feet higher than the 12th; Hankou 45.7 feet, 0.3 feet higher than the 12th; Jiujiang 43.4 feet, same as the 12th; Anqing 38.0 feet, same as the 12th.

(3) Lower reaches: Wuhu 27.3 feet, 0.1 feet lower than the 12th; Nanjing 21.6 feet, 0.1 feet lower than the 12th; Zhenjiang 8.0 feet, 0.5 feet lower than the 12th. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 13th)

(Hankou) The river water rose three inches on the 13th, with the water mark at 45 feet 7 inches, nine inches from the bank. Yisha rose six inches, Changsha rose eight inches, and Yuezhou rose one foot six inches. However, Chongqing receded seven inches, reducing the level of danger. The Provincial Flood Control Committee, noting the increasingly severe leakage in the Wufeng Dike, determined four emergency rescue measures on the 13th, to be implemented starting on the 14th, including the construction of a transverse dike as the second line of defense for flood prevention. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

(Nanjing) According to the Yangtze River Waterway Improvement Commission, the water level in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River has gradually receded, easing public anxiety. Wanxian has receded another eight feet. Based on the timing, the flood season for this month has passed. If the weather remains favorable, there should be no risk of a sudden surge within the month. However, the dikes in Anhui, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces have suffered breaches in several locations due to the inability to discharge internal water and the backflow of external water, resulting in the submersion of extensive farmland. The Flood Prevention Committee is currently intensifying its supervision of staff to expedite rescue efforts. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance has allocated an additional 50,000 yuan to the Yangtze River Flood Prevention Committee specifically for purchasing burlap sacks to be used in dike reinforcement projects. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

The Yellow River at Luokou Continues to Rise 38

All Critical Engineering Works Are Simultaneously Under Pressure

(Jinan) Today, the Yellow River at Luokou rose 2.7 decimeters, with the water level at 29.6 meters. At Dongzhuang in the upper reaches, the water rose 1.8 decimeters, nearing the highest water level of last year. All critical engineering works are simultaneously under pressure. Inspector Yang Zhenliang urgently reported on the night of the 12th that the tenth and fifth groynes of Li Shengtun in the upper reaches were submerged by about a foot. The seventh groyne had collapsed, with the front and rear sections at water level, making it difficult to maintain. By 11 PM, the top of the seventh groyne had eroded by more than two zhang both in front and behind, losing its shape. The River Affairs Bureau has telegraphed all county heads along the river today, urging them to quickly set up temporary shelters, supervise the district and village chiefs to diligently oversee the laborers, and cooperate with the assigned officials to defend the area. The bureau also telegraphed all river section chiefs and committee members to supervise the soldiers and laborers, patrol day and night, and defend the area as circumstances dictate. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

A Water Conservancy Expert Discusses the Avoidability of Floods in Jiangsu Province 39

No Increase in Huai River Levels, Nor Hurricanes

(Zhenjiang) Recently, water levels have risen sharply across the country, attracting extreme attention from the government and the people regarding flood prevention efforts. People in Jiangsu Province are particularly concerned about the canal, and the provincial government is also paying full attention to the matter. A Central News Agency reporter interviewed a water conservancy expert yesterday. According to him, based on academic and practical considerations, Jiangsu Province is unlikely to experience a flood disaster this year. The reasons are: (1) Jiangsu, bordering the Yangtze, Huai, Yi, Si, and Shu Rivers, is the downstream destination for all these waters, making the situation extremely serious. However, precisely because it is located at the end of the waterways, drainage is easier, making a disaster less likely. (2) The causes of floods in Jiangsu are the four elements of Yangtze River, Huai River, tides, and winds. A severe disaster occurs when the Yangtze and Huai Rivers rise simultaneously, coinciding with a period of high tides (around the new and full moon), and exacerbated by a hurricane passing through. The situation becomes exceptionally serious. Even a slight lapse in protection will lead to a major disaster. When the Huai River flows into the Yangtze (the waters south of the Yangtze also flow into the Yangtze, hence the similar situations north and south of the Yangtze), and both the Huai and Yangtze Rivers rise, the source becomes vast and the downstream is blocked. Internal and external pressures combine, causing water levels to rise significantly. If this is compounded by a tidal backflow, the Yangtze River water cannot easily flow into the sea, preventing the Yangtze River water level from dropping, creating a crisis situation. If a hurricane strikes, it will inevitably cause waves that batter the dikes, making defense even more difficult. If defenses are inadequate or the personnel are ineffective, it will lead to a disaster. (3) The prediction for this year's situation is that only one-fourth of the aforementioned conditions are present; that is, only the Yangtze River water level is high. Recently, due to a sudden increase in tides (the highest tide was on the 10th of this month), the waters in the upper and middle reaches have not receded easily. However, the Huai River water level has not risen, and there is no sign of a hurricane. Therefore, a disaster is unlikely. Furthermore, from now on, the tide level will fall daily, making water recession easier. Not only will Jiangsu Province be spared from the threat of Yangtze River flooding, but the middle and upper reaches of the Yangtze River can also be free from worry. Even if the Huai River were to rise again, it is estimated that the period of highest water level in the Yangtze River would only be extended by a maximum of twenty days. Half of that time has already passed. For the Huai River to rise to its maximum level, it would take at least ten days. Considering these factors, it can be concluded that there is no major threat. As for any breaches in the Yangtze River dikes, due to the terrain, the damage will only affect a small local area and will not impact the majority of Jiangsu Province. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 13th)

Strange Heat in Beiping 40

(Beiping) The city of Beiping experienced strange heat today. Yesterday it was 102 degrees, and today it is above 102 degrees. Heavy rain is expected tonight. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

Page 9

Awards for Articles on Party Ideology Review Committee

Organizational Rules and Review Rules 41

(Nanjing) The Central Standing Committee passed the organizational rules and review rules for the Awards for Articles on Party Ideology Review Committee on the 13th. The original text is as follows:

(A) Organizational Rules: (1) The Central Awards for Articles on Party Ideology Review Committee (hereinafter referred to as "the Committee") is established based on the resolution of the 68th Central Standing Committee regarding awards for articles on Party ideology. To facilitate review, it is organized by the directors of the Central Propaganda Committee and the Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee (hereinafter referred to as "the two Committee directors") who appoint several working colleagues from each committee. (2) The Committee does not interact externally but is directly under the two Committee directors, following their guidance to handle matters related to reviewing awards for articles on Party ideology. (3) The Committee will temporarily have twelve review members. In addition to the secretaries and section chiefs of the two committees, who will be ex officio review members, the two Committee directors will appoint four working colleagues from each committee to serve concurrently. Additional members may be added as needed. (4) The Committee will temporarily have two staff members, jointly selected by the two Committee directors, each from their respective committees, to handle Committee affairs. (5) The Committee will meet once a week and may convene temporary meetings as necessary. (6) The chair of the Committee meetings will be rotated between the secretaries or section chiefs of the two committees, who will be responsible for convening regular or temporary meetings and directing the staff. (7) The Committee may invite the two Committee directors to attend and provide guidance during important meetings. (8) Detailed working rules for the Committee will be formulated separately. (9) Any matters not covered by these rules may be proposed by the Committee to the two Committee directors for modification. (10) These rules will be implemented after approval by the two Committee directors and filing with the Central Executive Committee.

(B) Review Rules: (1) Upon receiving articles on Party ideology, the Central Awards for Articles on Party Ideology Review Committee shall have the outline or table of contents of said articles mimeographed in several copies for submission to the meeting for review. (2) The initial review shall be the responsibility of two review members designated by the meeting, with the principle of one member from each committee. Each person shall carefully review and sign their opinions within the prescribed time. (3) The follow-up review shall be conducted by the meeting based on the initial review opinions. If a further review is deemed necessary, another person may be appointed for a follow-up review, which shall be completed and signed with opinions within the prescribed time. The meeting shall then decide whether to award the article and the award level. (4) The review opinions decided by the Committee meeting, or those that cannot be decided, shall be presented in detail to the directors of the Central Propaganda Committee and the Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee for joint approval. (5) The review opinions decided by the Committee meeting, or those that cannot be decided, shall be signed by all attending review members when submitted to the two Committee directors for approval. (6) After the two Committee directors have approved the award method for the articles on Party ideology, the Committee shall, in the name of the two Committee directors, submit the award to the Central Executive Committee. (7) The deadline for Committee review members to review manuscripts shall be determined by the meeting. (8) These rules shall be implemented upon approval by the two Committee directors. Any matters not covered shall be amended by the two Committee directors or by the Committee proposing to the two Committee directors for modification. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 13th)

Italian Air Squadron Flies Across the Atlantic 66

Lands on a Peninsula in Canada

▲ Reuters, New Brunswick, 12th: The Italian air squadron arrived at Cartwright in Labrador at 12:30 PM today, completing the most difficult leg of its journey to Chicago. The next leg will be from Cartwright to Sazdes, a distance of only 750 miles, but navigation will be difficult. After arriving at Sazdes, they will fly another 500 miles to Montreal, and then to Chicago. When the Italian air squadron arrived here today, they came in groups of three to five. They began arriving at 3:10 PM, with several aircraft arriving every ten or forty minutes. The first aircraft was sighted at Cartwright at 1:50 PM.

▲ Kuo Min Agency, New York, 12th: A message received via Mackay Radio states that the Italian air squadron safely arrived at Cartwright in Labrador at noon today. All aircraft are intact. The first aircraft landed at 2:50 PM, and the last aircraft landed at 5:20 PM. It is reported that after departing from Iceland, they flew in groups of three, encountering no difficulties along the way. After a stopover in Montreal, they plan to proceed to Chicago.

▲ Havas, New Brunswick, 12th: We received a radio message stating that the air squadron led by Italian Air Minister General Balbo has flown across the Atlantic from Iceland and arrived at Cartwright in Labrador, Canada.

▲ Kuo Min Agency, Cartwright, 13th: After the Italian air squadron arrived here from Iceland, Italian Air Marshal Balbo stated that the journey was extremely dangerous. They encountered strong headwinds and extremely bad weather immediately after departure. The clouds were heavy and low, and the sky was dark. The aircraft had to fly close to the sea surface, making it impossible to follow a set route. After the fifth hour, they flew into dense fog. The pilots could hardly see the lights on their own wings. In addition, the water droplets on the wings were suspected to be freezing, so they did not dare to fly above 300 feet. When they flew out of the heavy fog, the weather was slightly better. From the tenth to the twelfth hour, the weather was clear and cloudless, but the sea was stormy and the wind was treacherous. Moreover, they encountered strong headwinds throughout the journey, with the maximum speed not exceeding 125 miles per hour, further increasing the difficulty of the flight. Due to the bad weather, the aircraft were scattered from the beginning. But when they arrived here, they were still able to form groups of three. The pilots have demonstrated their excellent skills on this journey.

Forest Fire in Finland 67

Extends Over Thousands of Square Miles

Several Places Were Arsoned

▲ Reuters, Helsinki, 12th: The drought in Finland has caused a large forest fire in the interior, extending over thousands of square miles. The harvest of agricultural products has also suffered significant losses. The people in the affected areas are assisting in the rescue efforts. It is reported that there are several places where the fire was deliberately set.

Rampant Kidnappings in the United States

Roosevelt Organizes Anti-Kidnapping Campaign 68

▲ Reuters, Washington, 12th: Since the end of Prohibition, mobsters have lost a source of income, leading to rampant kidnapping cases across the country. President Roosevelt is now organizing a large-scale anti-kidnapping campaign. Roosevelt has ordered state officials to cooperate in solving the kidnapping cases of New York Democratic Party leader Walker O'Connell's nephew and the famous financier Feike. The O'Connell family expects Walker to be released within twelve hours and is said to be paying a ransom of $100,000. The exact amount is unknown. However, according to today's report, the Walker family is currently negotiating with the kidnappers. It is also reported that Feike's kidnappers sent a reply to the Feike family demanding a ransom of $200,000. According to the Feike family, they have no way to raise the ransom. Ruhl, an elderly banker from Alton, Illinois, was also kidnapped on Monday night. His family is trying to contact the kidnappers because Ruhl is old and frail.

This Year's Soviet Financial Budget 69

The special characteristic of the Soviet financial budget is that it does not rely solely on tax revenue as its source of income. Instead, a significant portion of its income comes from the surplus of state-owned production enterprises. On the expenditure side, the largest portion is not allocated to government and military expenses, but rather to the expenses for operating various production, cultural, and construction projects. Therefore, the Soviet financial budget is essentially the culmination of the budgets of various production sectors, and its foundation is built on the budgets of industrial, agricultural, transportation, and other production enterprises. In addition, credit and social insurance are also important foundations. In other words, this budget is responsible for concentrating and allocating capital for the development of socialism and the economy, as well as concentrating funds from the people and allocating funds to the people. It is completely different from the financial budgets of capitalist countries. As for the agency responsible for formulating the budget, there is a special committee under the Central Executive Committee. This committee is responsible for formulating the central and federal financial budgets. The budgets of various departments form the basis for the central budget. As for local budgets, they are formulated by the local executive committees.

The financial budget for this year is described as follows: 1933 is the starting year of the second five-year plan, which is also the starting year of the second stage of development of the Soviet national economy. In this year's plan, the total industrial output value is expected to increase by 16.5% compared to last year. In terms of monetary value, the increase is 4.8 billion rubles (calculated at the prices of 1926-27).

In terms of railway transportation, it is expected that freight volume can be increased by 300 million tons, which is 12.5% in percentage terms. The total investment can reach 18 billion rubles. In terms of trade, capital can be increased by 6 billion rubles. The revenue and expenditure of the financial budget, which has been approved by the Budget and Financial Planning Department under the Central Executive Committee, is 35.011 billion rubles for revenue and 33.233 billion rubles for expenditure. Compared with 1932, the total budget has increased by 5 billion rubles (from 29.949 million to 35.011 million rubles), which is 16.9% in percentage terms. Under the expenditure items, there is no significant increase because there is a government surplus of 178 million rubles included.

(A) Revenue. The following table compares the revenue of 1932 and 1933:

1932　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　1933

Amount (million rubles) Percentage of total revenue　Amount (million rubles) Percentage of total revenue

Item

Socialization of the national economy　　24719　　82.5　　28749　　82.1

Centralized private capital　　　4373　　14.6　　5364　　15.3

Other (such as taxes)　　　　857　　2.9　　898　　2.6

Total　　　　　　　　　29949　　100.0　　35011　　100.0

There are two main sources of revenue from the socialized national economy. One is from commercial operations. The form of this income is business tax. The second is the surplus allocated to the government from various economic organizations, such as the surplus of industrial and agricultural enterprises, and the revenue of railways, post offices, telegraph lines, and radio telegraphs.

The income from business tax ranks first in the financial budget revenue, with a total of 21.8 billion rubles, or 62.4% of the total revenue. The increase in this tax revenue depends on the production situation and the commercial situation of those who are obligated to pay taxes. In addition, changes in the prices of industrial products and daily necessities may also affect the business tax of various goods. In the 1933 budget, the change in tax rates is minimal, so the average tax rate of 1932 can be maintained. The reason why the business tax in 1933 can be increased by 4.4 billion rubles compared to 1932 is due to the more prosperous tax-paying trade than before. The comparison is as follows: (unit: million rubles)

Year　　　　Total number of tax-paying trades　　Tax amount　　　Average tax rate in percentage

1932　　43817　　17227　　39.3

1933　　54721　　21796　　39.7

Percentage of 1933 to 1932　　124.9　　136.8　　101.0

If the tax levied after the sale of special products calculated according to the selling price of 1932 is included in the revenue item of the previous budget, the total revenue can reach 23.5 billion rubles, or 67.2% of the total revenue. From this, it can be seen that two-thirds of the revenue must be transferred according to the situation of the national commodity trade. Fortunately, the market demand is very high. It is estimated that the 16.5% increase in industrial products in 1933 will not be able to meet the needs of the people and the socialized sector.

The second most important source of revenue in the budget is the accumulation of industry, credit institutions, and transportation. The total accumulation of the socialized sector is determined to be 20.2 billion rubles. The source of this total accumulation is to intensify production, increase freight volume, reduce the cost of industrial products, and increase the production capacity of workers according to the plan. Of this accumulation, 3.9 billion must be included in the financial budget revenue.

The second item in the budget revenue is tax revenue, which is the tax paid by the people, or the free contribution fee. The tax paid by the people is income tax. Those who pay this tax are workers and employees who are hired at high prices, as well as people who do not work but have income (owners of industrial and commercial enterprises, etc.). As for donations, they are used to subsidize the development of cultural and social undertakings. In addition, there are also donations to offset the tax amount that farmers who can only work but cannot pay taxes should pay. The total amount of this tax revenue is 215.2 million rubles, which is 6.1% of the total revenue. The second item of revenue increased by 38 million rubles compared to last year. The reason for the increase is the increase in the wages and salaries of employees in various national economic sectors, the increase in agriculture, and the increase in the number of workers.

The people's free donations raised in the form of reasonable government bonds are very important in terms of income. A part of economic construction is carried out by raising government bonds from the people. In recent years, due to the rapid progress of economic construction, the people's lives have become more stable due to the progress and expansion of economic construction. This phenomenon is tantamount to a solid barrier to the state's guarantee of government bonds. Therefore, whenever the government issues government bonds, the people are eager to subscribe. The government's debt, as of January 1, 1933, was 6.5 billion rubles. With the addition of various government bonds that must be raised again in 1933, the total amount by January 1, 1934, should reach 9 billion rubles. As for the relationship between government bonds and the people, it should be judged by the number of bondholders. The number of people in the Soviet Union who purchased government bonds was 8 million in 1928, 12 million in 1930, and increased to 40 million in 1932. The amount of government bonds allocated to the budget revenue item is 321.2 million rubles, which is 9.3% of the revenue.

In other aspects of income, there are a total of 500 million rubles in 1933. This is the subsidy from the highest social insurance agency for university scholarships. The reason why this amount is included in the budget is to make the calculation of scholarships simpler. The scholarships allocated by the social insurance agency actually only account for a portion of the total amount, and other parts still need to find other ways to inject funds. In addition, there are miscellaneous items in the income item, such as miscellaneous taxes (140 million rubles), and the amount transferred to the government from freight and passenger revenue (18.3 million rubles), etc. (To be continued)

### Large Bribery Case in Kyoto, Japan 70

Those Indicted are all Prominent Figures

Among them, Three Suspicions are the Most Important

According to the Nagoya Shimbun, due to the expansion of business in Kyoto City, illegal activities have continuously occurred between city officials, merchants in and out of the city, and contractors. Since Showa 3 (1928), the Kyoto Prefectural Criminal Investigation Division has obtained various scandals. It was not until March 16 of this year that conclusive evidence was obtained. After three months of investigation by the Kyoto District Public Prosecutors Office, 68 people who accepted and offered bribes were successively indicted. These criminals are all prominent figures such as senior officials, councilors, city councilors, and industrialists in Kyoto City, such as Minseito (Democratic Constitutional Party) councilor Kawahashi, Seiyukai (Friends of Constitutional Government) councilor Suzuki, city councilor Yagi, city government section chiefs, officers, engineers, and secretaries, who colluded with each other. Among them, there are three major suspicions that can be specially written about, namely, 1) the Nikiseki (Japan Oil) incident, in which Seiyukai councilors colluded with engineers and Japan Oil Company to bribe 20,000 yen for road construction; 2) the Funayama incident, in which oil merchant Funakoshi received several thousand yen in bribes for land readjustment; 3) the Daiichi Kogyo (First Industry) incident, in which councilor Suzuki received 6,000 yen in bribes to acquire the foundation of the Daiichi Kogyo school. Other incidents such as extorting thank-you money and accepting goods are too numerous to mention. Such a scandalous incident is truly the biggest stain in the history of Kyoto City.

### Various Parties' Movements After the Coup in Xinjiang Province 71

Sheng Shicai is Wary of the Examples of Usurpation and His Subordinates are Causing Trouble

Huang Musong's Safety is Absolutely Not a Problem

The Central Government will have a Great Plan to Develop the Border Areas

Beijing News: After the second coup in Xinjiang Province, the central government is painstakingly planning and preparing, but after half a month, it is still unclear. According to related parties, the actual situation has been obtained, and the outline is described below for those who are concerned about the Xinjiang Province incident to refer to.

Reasons for the Second Coup 72

It was found that when the first Xinjiang coup broke out on April 12, the initiators who opposed Jin Shuren were actually Tao Mingyue, Chen Zhong, and a small number of lower-ranking military officers. Due to the deep resentment of the people, Jin fled in a panic. At that time, Sheng Shicai was confronting Ma Zhongying's troops in Jichang (about a hundred miles away from Dihua). Upon hearing the news, he rushed back. After a few days, under the guidance of Tao and Chen, he was elected by the People's Congress to appoint Sheng Shicai and Liu Wenlong to lead the military and political affairs, and the matter came to an end. Tao and Chen were the key figures in the new coup. After Sheng took over as the Border Defense Commissioner, he was wary of the examples of usurpation in Xinjiang Province in the past. Tao and Chen, relying on their merits, were arrogant and indulgent, and things were unavoidable. Therefore, mutual suspicion deepened, and the cause of the second coup was conceived. When the central government specially sent Huang Musong as the envoy of comfort, if he had immediately started the festival, traveled lightly and simply, and flew to Dihua, Ma Zhongying would have no intention of trying again, and Liu Sheng might not have excessive thoughts. At that time, it would have been impossible to take advantage of the situation. Unfortunately, Huang recruited talents and prepared for the economy, and his actions were delayed. When he arrived in Xinjiang Province, it was when Tao and Chen were harboring their hopes. Tao and others flattered Huang as a senior member of the central government, which was the strength of a villain. Huang had no other thoughts in his heart, but Sheng and Liu became more and more worried. Therefore, based on one-sided actions, killing Tao was not enough, and they suspected that Huang had the intention of taking away their power.

After Jiang and Wang's Public Telegrams 73

After the central government received Liu Shengjian's telegram report, the director of the province's Beijing office, Zhang Fengjiu, and the party affairs instructor, Peng Zhaoxian, sent telegrams to Liu Sheng, explaining the central government's attitude and inquiring about the truth of the incident. As for the public telegrams issued by Chairman Chiang and President Wang, due to the distance, it would take until around the 20th to receive a reply. However, Peng Zhaoxian recently received another telegram from Sheng, which stated, "In this Xinjiang coup, I was forced by the environment to maintain the situation. The rumors are untrue, which is a pity. I welcome Wenjing's visit to the west and hope to come soon to be encouraged. As for the Xinjiang incident, it was purely caused by Ma bandits causing chaos. Now Ma bandits have led the remnants of six or seven hundred people to collapse and retreat to Shanshan. I am preparing to pursue them in order to thoroughly eliminate them. If Ma bandits are eliminated, then everything will be solved easily." This situation has been telegraphed to Chairman Chiang." After receiving the telegram, Peng sent another telegram to encourage Liu Sheng's attitude of always obeying the central government and to pay attention to the safety of Huang, the envoy of comfort, again and again. Respecting Huang is respecting the central government, and it is explained that Huang's visit to Xinjiang has absolutely no intention of usurping power, and it is hoped that there will be no further misunderstandings. Regarding all the aftermath, it will be discussed in detail after the new situation is reached. This telegram was sent the day before yesterday.

The Central Government's Attitude Towards Handling the Situation 74

The general cause of the second coup in Xinjiang Province has been described above. What attitude will the central government hold in the future? This is what the general public urgently wants to know. According to the opinions of various military and political authorities, President Wang reported in the Administrative Yuan Memorial Weekly a few days ago (Monday) that "the three things mentioned in the Xinjiang incident, namely, first, diplomacy must be unified under the central government; second, military affairs must be unified under the central government; and third, religion must be free and ethnic groups must be equal. These three are the major goals of the future administration of Xinjiang, and they are also the crystallization of Wang Jiang's exchange of telegrams to deal with the new changes in the past half month. If Liu Sheng expresses a clear compliance with this, and Huang Musong has not suffered excessive embarrassment in Xinjiang, then the order to remove Liu Sheng from his position will not be clearly seen. As for the effective development of Xinjiang Province in the future, the central government has recently had detailed discussions in a high-level meeting, and there is a strong momentum for it to be implemented. The scope is heard not only limited to Xinjiang Province, but it should be the second step in the plan to administer Xinjiang."

Peng and Gong's Departure is Near 75

After the second change in Xinjiang, President of the Executive Yuan Wang Jingwei summoned Zhang Fengjiu and Gong Bicheng to inquire about ways to quell the chaos, and instructed Gong to return to Xinjiang with Peng Zhaoxian to investigate the truth. At the same time, he ordered Huang, the envoy of comfort, to return to Beijing as soon as possible. However, as of today, Gong and Peng's departure date has been postponed, and Huang's return is undecided. The truth of the matter is enough to make people speculate. Yesterday, Peng Zhaoxian said, "President Wang did talk to Mr. Gong at one time and instructed me to go to Xinjiang immediately, but my office has never received a formal order, so I have not been able to make the trip. If the central government does have this intention, I will certainly comply. However, the party affairs instructor Cao Qiwen has already taken a plane to Xinjiang yesterday (11th) morning. Once Mr. Cao arrives, he will first report the recent situation of the province here. Whether the departure date is still pending. Yesterday, Dong Shuizhen and Yang Mengzhou, two of Sheng's acquaintances, also went to Xinjiang together. Dong was invited by Sheng's telegram. Also, Mr. Wang Ziyao, the representative of Li Du, also took the same plane to Xinjiang." Peng said at the end that the safety of Huang, the envoy of comfort, he guarantees will definitely not be a problem, because Huang and Sheng have very friendly personal relations. Even if there is a slight misunderstanding in the public aspect, it will soon be dispelled.

Zhang Fengjiu Returned to Beijing Yesterday 76

Zhang Fengjiu, director of the Xinjiang Office in Beijing, returned to Beijing yesterday (12th) after being summoned to Ganzhou by Chairman Chiang a few days ago. According to Zhang, "I was summoned to Ganzhou this time and transferred to Mount Lu, where I met Chairman Chiang. Chiang paid unusual attention to the Xinjiang incident and inquired in detail. However, because he was busy with the work of suppressing bandits, he ordered me to return to Beijing first to meet President Wang and said that the detailed measures had been telegraphed to Wang and all the problems could be solved in Beijing. Therefore, after arriving in Beijing by plane at 10 o'clock this morning, I went to see President Wang and received instructions from the central government on the intention to resolve the Xinjiang incident, and immediately ordered Gong Bicheng and Peng Zhaoxian to go to Xinjiang to mediate the disputes, with the principle of taking into account the prestige of the central government and complying with local public opinion. What names the two will go in is currently being discussed, and it will probably be announced within a few days. They will set off when the Eurasia plane departs next Tuesday. The order to remove Liu Sheng from the position of chairman and governor of Xinjiang Province will be decided after Gong and Peng arrive in Xinjiang." He also said that Liu Sheng's emergency resolution of the internal changes in the Xinjiang Provincial Government and the execution of Tao, Chen, and Li were entirely because Tao and others attempted a riot, so he had no choice but to deal with it in this way. As for the central government officials, he absolutely supports them. The various rumors outside may not be reliable.

Outline of Liu Sheng's Resume 77

The current situation in Xinjiang Province is that Sheng and Liu are responsible for the military and political power. Therefore, the experience of the two and their prestige in Xinjiang, as well as their relationship with the central government, seem to have the value of being recorded. It is found that Liu Wenlong is old and has served as an official in Xinjiang Province for more than 30 years. He usually handles things and is still popular with the people, so he has the reputation of Liu Qingtian. In the past, due to his position, he rarely approached the central government, and few people knew about him and his actions. Sheng Shicai graduated from the Japanese Army University. After returning to China, he served as the lieutenant colonel section chief of the General Headquarters here in the 17th year of the Republic of China. He had great talent. In the year, the central government participated in the military opportunities for the Feng and Yan campaigns. Gu Yao Chiang's Commander in Chief gave Qing. In the 19th year of the Republic of China, through the introduction of Peng Zhaobao, the current party affairs instructor of Xinjiang Province, he went to Xinjiang to serve as the chief of the staff office of the Border Defense Governor's Office. At first, he had no name. Until Ma Zhongying rebelled against Jin for the first time in the past (Shuren), Jin's troops were defeated. Sheng took the opportunity to offer suggestions and set a date and place to quell the Ma chaos. Jin Yun's request was then granted the position of acting chief of staff and granted full power. As a result, everything was as expected and the turmoil was quelled as scheduled. Jin was greatly appreciated and truly removed the chief and concurrently served as the president of the military school in the province. Since then, all matters related to the military have been planned by Sheng, and the potential power has gradually increased. This time, he has gained military power. Sheng is 37 this year and studied under Chairman Chiang and Huang Musong, the envoy of comfort, who were originally classmates. (Daily News)

Chiang is Temporarily Stationed in Mount Lu 78

Visited Fuzhou

Currently Planning to Establish a Mountain Climbing School

Fuzhou Correspondence: Since Zhu Mao shifted their target from southern Jiangxi to eastern Jiangxi the year before last, Fuzhou has become the military center for suppressing the Red Army. Moreover, the false 135th Army Corps has repeatedly needed to attack northward in full force, hoping to seize Fuzhou in order to enter Naxun and break through the Yangtze River. At the beginning of last month, Zhu Mao personally led the false 452nd and other armies of Lin Biao, Luo Binghui, and Dong Zhentang, protruding from Yihuang upstream of the Fu River and invading the suburbs of Fuzhou. The momentum was fierce. Chairman Chiang considered that the Red bandits had left their nests and penetrated deeply, and it was necessary to take advantage of the opportunity to severely suppress them. Therefore, on the 19th, after attending the county magistrate's meeting and giving instructions, he took a car on the Ganmin Road to Fuzhou and stationed in the Eighth Middle School, working in the Governor's Office set up by Liu Zhi a few days ago. Chiang's arrival in Fuzhou was also to personally serve as the commander of the Northern Route Army to direct military affairs on the front line. After Chiang arrived in Fuzhou, he immediately summoned various generals to give instructions, gave face-to-face instructions, and limited the immediate advance to Yihuang. At that time, the various departments in eastern Jiangxi were encouraged by Chiang's personal supervision, and their morale was boosted. They immediately drove the bandits who had invaded the vicinity of Fuzhou out of the country and lifted the siege of Yihuang on the 25th. In addition to visiting Nancheng Chongren and Yihuang, Chiang also repeatedly summoned Li Siqiu and other departments who had newly arrived in Fuzhou to give instructions, encouraging them to work hard to eliminate the bandit scourge. It is estimated that about five or six divisions of people have been added to Jiangxi from other provinces in the past month. They have all been concentrated in Kou and opened to the Koukou front line. Therefore, the various departments in Yihuang followed the bandits and have reached Koukou and other places south of Yihuang. Zhu Mao's main force retreated to the areas bordering Yile and Ningdu, such as Zhaoxie, Dongbi, Xiaotian, Huangpi, and Xiaopu. According to information from various sources, Zhu Mao used the five provinces to encircle them in three routes, and the date of death has arrived. They are currently discussing countermeasures and discussing each other's claims. 1) Attack Fuzhou with all their strength; 2) Take Fang Shao as the vanguard and flee east to western Zhejiang to build a new nest; 3) Attack Ji'an in the west or Ganzhou in the south to seize the central city. The opinions of the bandits are divided, so there is no decision. Recently, they are still lurking in the dangerous mountainous areas south of Huangpi. The various departments in eastern Jiangxi have strictly sealed off the bandit areas south of Yile Chong and set up defenses on dangerous terrain. Once the Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian armies have captured Tingzhou and Huichang, they will simultaneously divide into routes to Ningdu for encirclement. Chiang, having made arrangements in Fuzhou, urgently needed to deal with military affairs in the rear, and returned to the province on the 6th.

After Chiang returned to the province, considering that the bandits have used the complex mountains and rugged roads to seek long-term defense, he decided to train lower-level officers for mountain warfare in order to command. Therefore, there is the establishment of a mountain climbing school. It is said that the school site is selected on the southern foot of Mount Lu, and the students are selected from the Central Military Academy and lower-level officers, and after training, they are transferred to the front line as a vanguard for suppressing bandits in mountain warfare. Therefore, Chiang took a Ford aircraft from the province to Jiujiang on the afternoon of the 9th of this month and transferred to Mount Lu to preside over everything. The school will be officially opened soon. (July 10)

Jiading

Dispute Over Change of Heads of Public Security Sub-bureaus 83

Yang Geseng, the head of the county Public Security Bureau, recently transferred the heads of the Waigang and Loutang Public Security Sub-bureaus. After receiving the order, Jin Jisheng, the head of the Waigang Sub-bureau, handed over his duties and went to Loutang in September to take over. Pan Jixiang, the head of the Loutang Sub-bureau, was on leave, and Secretary Feng Yifei informed Jin that he should wait for Pan to return to the bureau and hand over the duties in person, as he could not act without authorization. Jin insisted on taking over immediately, causing a dispute that reached outside the bureau. Tang Wenpei, the head of the Baoan Corps, and others rushed to the scene upon hearing the commotion and persuaded Jin not to argue. Jin, considering Tang's words to be biased, accused him of being the mastermind. The Baoan Corps then gathered all the members of the town's militia and marched to Jin to question him. The incident was finally calmed down by Mei Zude, the fifth district chief, who rushed to mediate. Jin, unable to take over despite the order, returned to the county bureau to complain. Director Yang left the bureau for Shanghai the same day, as the mutual transfer of the sub-bureau chiefs had not been approved by the county government. The dispute has not yet been resolved. Zhou Jing and others in Loutang Town have jointly petitioned the county government to reduce the scope of the bureau and save expenses.

Supervisory Office Hires Advisors 84

Xu Weizhen, the administrative supervisor of the sixth district, has hired Zhang Gongquan, Jin Jushan, Jin Houcheng, Wang Jianbin, Gu Zhenyi, Zhao Housheng, Mr. Bao from Baoshan; Xia Ri'ao, Wang Quanshi, Pan Zhixing, Huang Yusun, Jin Boqin, Gu Jisheng, Yang Weiyu from Jiading; Tang Wenzhi, Hong Baoping, Zhu Kaichou, Wu Shengsan, Qian Yi, Jiang Yuren, Wang Qihua, and other twenty-one people from Taicang as advisors to the Supervisory Office.

Wujiang

County Water Patrol Team Repeatedly Captures Prominent Bandits 85

In the past two days, the county water patrol team has successively captured many notorious bandits. Li San confessed to robbing Chen Yunzhong's family in Dongzang Township, the fifth district, and kidnapping Pan Shouchang and his daughter Pan Aizhen in the tenth district for ransom, as well as tearing up Pan Shouchang's ticket, intercepting firearms from various water police units in Jiaxing, Xinji, and Dongshan, and killing police officers. Zheng Guoxiang confessed to kidnapping Lu, the daughter-in-law of Wu Jinhe's family in Xiaoligang Village, Liucan Township, the ninth district, as well as Sun Sijin. Zheng Quanfu (aka Zheng San), Liu Hanchen, Cao Yaoguang (aka Cao Dazui), and Lei Xiaoheizi all confessed to robbing Zhang Jinfu's family in Changtiangang, Bailong Bridge, as well as a monk from Donglin Temple, and tearing up the monk's ticket. They also confessed to kidnapping two female hostages in Bazhuang Township, Pan Wangpo's family in Kuilianggang, the tenth district, and kidnapping Pan Shouchang and his daughter Pan Aizhen in the tenth district for ransom, killing Pan Shouchang when the ransom was not paid, intercepting thirteen firearms from various ships and water police units, and shooting police officers, as well as robbery cases on Wujiang boats and at the Jade Emperor Temple. These bandits were all accomplices of the executed Geng Mazi and Wang Guangheng. There are still fugitives at large, and efforts are being made to capture them. The capture of this large number of bandit leaders has greatly pleased the residents.

Changshu

Insane Woman Accuses Husband of Colluding with Bandits 86

At around 2 PM on the 10th, a woman in her forties, weeping bitterly, rushed to the first court of the county government, claiming to have an important case to report and requesting the magistrate to open the court. Her attempts to stop were unsuccessful, and the trial was presided over by Huang. According to the woman's statement, her name was Lu Qian, 47 years old, residing at Tajiao Bridge outside Xiaodongmen. Her husband, Song Song, was colluding with bandits at home. Every night, many people would enter and exit her house. Her husband's bed had a hidden mechanism, with a hemp rope connected directly to the outside, one end tied to a brick and the other to his body. If someone activated it, her husband would get up to greet them. She had repeatedly advised him to stop, but he had beaten her. Fearing future trouble, she had come to report. If they did not believe her, they could inspect her house, she said. Judge Huang, according to her statement, found the matter strange and immediately dispatched bailiffs to secretly detain Lu Songsong at the county. He also went to Lu's house to investigate. The neighbors all gossiped, generally saying that Lu was honest, and that Qian may have a mental illness, as she had been seen at the Public Security Bureau many times. After Songsong arrived at the county, the county government questioned him again. Qian still claimed that her husband was a kidnapper. In the first year of the Republic, he had been detained for robbing rice. When questioned, Lu Songsong claimed to be 57 years old, making paper lanterns for a living, and was usually peaceful and dared not collude with bandits. What his wife said was completely false. At this point, Songsong's son, Lu Shengzai, also turned himself in, claiming that his mother had a mental illness and her statement should not be believed. As a result, the court ordered Lu Songsong to be released on bail, pending further investigation by the Public Security Bureau.

Bureau of Education Replaces Large Number of Principals 87

Every year at the end of the academic year, the Bureau of Education is required to reappoint principals. However, the education sector here is divided by factions, making it difficult to handle affairs. This year, the Bureau of Education dismissed twenty-four principals. The successors have not yet been announced. The principals of the larger schools in the county have been appointed first, including Zhu Yinli, principal of the Rural Normal School, Sun Gongyuan, principal of the County Middle School, Yang Junhe, principal of the Shimei Elementary School, Liu Gongpu, principal of the Xigang Elementary School, and Tong Shizhong, principal of the Bailingcang Elementary School.

Wuxi

Silk Filature Industry Asks for Reduction or Exemption of Business Tax 88

The Silk Filature Industry Association of this county received letters yesterday from members such as Qia Changxiang, Xie Xing and other silk filatures, as well as Xu Shaowen and other silk firms, stating that the local Business Tax Bureau has sent personnel to various firms, setting deadlines for filling out declaration forms and implementing taxation. However, each firm already holds a broker's license, which is called a business license, and the tax collected is called a business tax. Now, the Business Tax Bureau is imposing taxes again, which is tantamount to double taxation for one industry. After the decline of the silk and cocoon industry, it is really unbearable. They requested the county Chamber of Commerce to strive for their benefit. At the same time, the association also received letters from Li Zhaoji, Wang Yansheng, and other raw silk factories, stating that the silk and cocoon industry has failed for many years, and the current business tax rate of 0.2% based on last year's revenue is already difficult to bear. However, the Business Tax Bureau has recently increased the business tax rate to 0.5%, which is really unbearable. They also requested the county Chamber of Commerce to strive for maintaining the original rate of 0.2%. After approving the letters, the association immediately forwarded them to the county Chamber of Commerce, requesting them to strive for the industry's benefit with the Business Tax Bureau.

Three Deaths Occur in One Day 89

Hua Guoxiang, a doorman at the Lixin Cloth Factory outside the North Gate, Huishang Bridge, 46 years old, a native of this county, has been working as a doorman at the factory for five or six years. He has not married and has quite a lot of savings. This year, during the Spring Festival, Hua used his savings to gamble, losing more than one hundred yuan. Afterwards, he became depressed, thinking about his years of savings being wasted in one day, and his nerves became abnormal. Recently, Hua suddenly had the thought of ending his life. At around 3 AM the night before, he sneaked into the factory's woodworking room and hanged himself. By the time he was discovered, he had already died. The town chief Huang Xisan of the 16th Tu reported the incident to the county court for inspection. The inspector, led by Prosecutor Ren, confirmed that it was a case of suicide by hanging. The factory handled the body with a coffin. Also, Ma Xilao, a resident of Zhongqiao Town, Yangming Township, the third district, over 70 years old, was scolded by his daughter-in-law Hu for a trivial matter a few days ago, and she threw feces on his face. Xilao was blind and unable to dodge. After being humiliated, he hanged himself at home behind people's backs yesterday. His son Helang is now handling the funeral arrangements. Also, Chen Guofa, a worker at the Yu Socks Factory in Xianlitun outside the West Gate, went swimming in the nearby ice pond on the afternoon of the day before, due to the hot weather. However, Chen was not a good swimmer and drowned. Yesterday, Zhang Jintai, the town chief of the 23rd and 5th Tu in the area, reported the incident to the court for inspection. Also, Shi Rong, a water carrier from Jiangbei who worked in Donghetou Alley in the city, was walking with a water bucket on his shoulder yesterday morning when an electric wire in the area fell in the wind, hitting Shi on the head. Shi tried to resist with his left hand, but upon contact, he immediately fell to the ground, unconscious. Fortunately, Sun Hanquan, a resident of the area, saw him and immediately hired a car to send him to the Guangfumen Sanatorium for treatment. However, his left hand was severely burned, and his brain was violently shocked, leaving him in a coma and in critical condition.

Jiangyin

Case of Robbery of Pig Boat on Linghu Lake Cracked 90

The Taohuagang in this county and the Dajuegang in the eighth district of Jingjiang have a public ferry, with Shen Chaoxiang as the ferry leader. The day before, the leader contacted Zhang Fusheng of Taohuagang and robbed 93 large pigs from a Linghu pig trader at the port, tying up the pig trader and releasing him in the weirs. Later, the pig trader reported to the Guazhou Water Police Headquarters, which ordered the 20th Brigade of this county to investigate. On the 6th, the water police captured Shen Chaoxiang's brother and brought him to the brigade headquarters for interrogation.

Order to Investigate Zhang Yipeng's Accusation 91

The county Party headquarters and various sectors initiated the construction of the Zhongshan Hall on the site of the former Mi Luo Pavilion, which was destroyed in the Xuanmiao Temple. Construction has already begun. However, Yan Juecang, the abbot of the Xuanmiao Temple, fearing that various miscellaneous items in the temple would be driven out after the Zhongshan Hall was built, which would greatly affect his income, filed a complaint with the Jiangsu Provincial People's Office, accusing Zhang Yipeng, the director of the preparatory committee, of destroying historical sites and encroaching on temple property. The Civil Affairs Office ordered the county to investigate and reply. The county government yesterday submitted the process of initiating the construction to the Civil Affairs Office for approval.

Zhenjiang

Water Level in Canal Continues to Drop 92

The upstream of the Jiangbei Canal was scoured by the waters of the Huai, Yi, and Hongze Lakes, while the downstream was pushed up by the rising tide, rising several feet. The water flow was rapid and overflowing. Xu Dingkang, the director of the Canal Engineering Bureau of Northern Jiangsu, released all the dams leading to the sea, fearing that the canal embankment would be in danger. The water level gradually dropped. According to the latest report, the water levels in Qingjiang, Gaoyou, Jiangdu, and other sections have all dropped by more than two feet.

Two Bookstores Burned Down Due to Carelessness 93

Zhonghe Bookstore is located at No. 41 Zhongshan Road, and No. 40 next door is Baicheng Bookstore. The houses there are all owned by Hong Bai. At around 1 AM yesterday, Zhonghe Bookstore caught fire due to an electrical fault and was suddenly burned down. After discovering the fire, the store originally hoped to extinguish it themselves, without making a sound, so as to avoid the books and goods being soaked in water. When the patrol police saw smoke coming from the bookstore and broke down the door, the fire had already spread. Zhang Yaoqing and others from Baicheng Bookstore helped to put out the fire, but it was impossible to control. The fire brigade rushed to the scene, but could not extinguish the fire except for the nearby Bank of China, Mei Hua Shoe Store, and He Quanwai. The Zhonghe and Baicheng bookstores were completely destroyed. However, in the chaos, Zhou Xiandong, the small shopkeeper of Zhonghe Bookstore, escaped with the account book and was detained by the police at the bureau. After interrogation by Pan, the director of the Second Branch Bureau, Zhou Renxi, the major shareholder of Zhonghe Bookstore, Chen Xianting, the small shareholder and manager, and Zhang Yaocheng, the manager of Baicheng Bookstore, testified that the fire in Zhonghe Bookstore was indeed caused by an electrical fault. Zhonghe lost about 10,000 yuan, and Baicheng lost about 5,000 yuan including goods. After hearing the testimony, Director Pan, considering that neither bookstore was insured and that it was a natural disaster, ordered them to provide proper guarantees and released them temporarily. Zhonghe Bookstore has set up a temporary office at the Huayang Hotel to handle the aftermath.

Qingjiang

Antiques Unearthed Outside the South Gate of the City 96

Su Yizi, a tiler outside the South Gate of Huaiyin City, near the old city river, has recently seen his business decline. At 3 PM on the 10th, he was building a toilet behind his house when he discovered a jar mouth in the soil, less than a foot deep. Su carefully investigated and found a large black ancient porcelain jar with a wide mouth. He then unearthed Qinghua plates, bowls, and several white porcelain ancient incense burners. The news spread quickly, and many people came to watch. Su, considering the unexpected event, has collected the excavated ancient porcelain and stopped working.

Also, the first battalion of the regiment stationed in Yugou Town presented a complaint from Liu Zheng of Wu Village, stating that her son Liu Qingzhao was imprisoned in a cellar by the bandit Wu Fengbao and suffocated to death. She requested the arrest of the murderer. The battalion arrested Wu Fengbao, who confessed to the crime. He was also sentenced to death by Commander Chen with approval. On the morning of the 10th, Regiment Commander Liu Zhongqi sent the bandits to Shunheji and Yugou for execution by firing squad.

Bengbu

No More Bandits in the Upper Reaches of the Changhuai River 99

There have been frequent bandit alarms in the upper reaches of the Changhuai River in recent months, and travelers have been wary. Bandits were previously discovered in Shitoubu, Fengtai County, robbing merchants and travelers. The Changhuai River Water Public Security Bureau, considering that the bandits' activities hindered water security, specially sent Director Wang Qi from Bengbu to lead a commando battalion to suppress them. After receiving the order, Wang led the team and set off, heading west by ship. The bandits, hearing that the water police were coming to suppress them, knew it would be difficult to stand their ground and fled. Therefore, when the team passed through Tianjiamiao, Shitoubu, and Fengtai County, the area was peaceful as usual, and there were no bandits. Wang then led the team upstream and arrived at Zhengyangguan, where he met Xu Zhongyue, the brigade commander of the 40th Independent Brigade of the stationed army, to discuss defense issues. However, since the bandits had already fled far away, there was no need to stay there for long. Yesterday, he led the team back to Bengbu and reported the situation of the patrol.

Local News

Ministry of Railways Prepares for Direct Train Service Between Beijing and Shanghai 100

Since the Ministry of Railways organized a preparatory committee for the direct train service between the Beijing-Shanghai and Tianjin-Pukou railways and actively carried out planning, concrete measures have been drafted for various procedures. After another meeting and discussion, it was formally decided to move the Changjiang Hao Xiaguan ferry, which was staying in Shanghai, to Beijing for installation. The following is a record of the relevant news:

Proposed Principles for Through Train Service 101

The preparatory committees for the Beijing-Shanghai and Tianjin-Pukou railways were jointly established by personnel from the Ministry of Railways and representatives from the Tianjin-Pukou and Beijing-Shanghai railways. Another meeting was convened to discuss the management of the ferry and the preparation for the direct train service between the two railways. Regarding the through train service, the committee has now proposed the following three principles: (1) From the date of the official through train service between the Beijing-Shanghai and Tianjin-Pukou railways, a direct passenger train will run between Shanghai and Beijing daily (schedule to be determined). (2) A total of seven passenger trains (number of cars to be determined) will be drawn from each railway, dedicated to the Shanghai-Beijing through train service. (3) The trains to be allocated by each railway should be proportional to the mileage of each railway, with five trains from Tianjin-Pukou, one from Beining, and one from Beijing-Shanghai. (The above measures were proposed by the Through Train Preparatory Committee, but the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration felt that there was a shortage of vehicles on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, so they have submitted a request to the Ministry of Railways to borrow three third-class passenger cars from the Jiaoji Railway, two second-class passenger cars from the Pinghan Railway, and three freight cars from the two railways themselves, which will be combined to form a train.) The above three principles will be submitted to the Ministry of Railways for approval and implementation within the next few days.

Stipulated Ferry Ticket Price 102

As for the passenger ferry ticket price, the Through Train Preparatory Committee decided that the Xiaguan River surface is ten li (actually only six or seven li), with first and second class tickets at 30 cents, and third and fourth class tickets at 17 cents. The freight rate for goods is 1.5 yuan per ton from Nanjing to Pukou upstream and 2 yuan per ton from Pukou to Nanjing downstream. However, the maximum at one time shall not exceed 1,200 tons. However, the railway authorities believe that this method is likely to be opposed by passengers and merchants, because the goods are transported on the same ferry, and the river crossing fee should not be charged differently for upstream and downstream, which will affect the direct freight transport of the Beijing-Shanghai and Tianjin-Pukou railways. In order to reduce the burden on passengers and merchants, it has recently instructed the Preparatory Committee to reduce the freight rate for goods crossing the river as much as possible within the possible range, and to abolish the names of upstream and downstream, and charge the same fee.

Ferry Management Matters 103

As for the management of the Changjiang Hao ferry, the Ministry of Railways has instructed the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Bureau to be responsible for handling it. The Tianjin-Pukou side has a port affairs section, and there are very good warehouses on both sides of the river, which are very convenient for loading and unloading goods on the ferry. The Nanjing freight yard of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway is located next to the Xiaguan Station, which is very far from the Changjiang Hao ferry terminal. Loading and unloading are inconvenient, and transshipment will take more time. Therefore, the Ministry of Railways handed over the management of the ferry to the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Bureau.

The Difficulties of Rescued Passengers and Crew of the Sunken Tunan

Japanese Refuse to Carry Crew Members 104

Fifty-three crew members and thirty-six passengers rescued by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Tunan ship arrived in Dalian at 10 AM on the 11th. Because they were waiting for the head office to send a ship to pick them up, the eighty-nine rescued crew members and passengers had been staying in Dalian for three days. The Shanghai office first sent a letter to the Dalian Steamship Company, requesting that a ship be sent to carry these rescued crew members and passengers to Shanghai, or to take the company's Dalian-Shanghai liner to Shanghai. However, the company did not reply to the letter sent on the 10th. Then the bureau sent someone to negotiate, but the Shanghai Dalian Steamship Company pushed the responsibility to the head office and refused to load these rescued crew members and passengers to Shanghai.

Xinfeng Sails to Dalian 105

Liu Hongsheng originally did not order the Xinfeng to go to Dalian to pick up the crew members. However, because the Japanese merchants had clearly refused the bureau's request to carry eighty-nine people to Shanghai, he had to telegraph the Xinfeng ship, which was going south from Tianjin, to sail to Dalian to pick up these crew members and passengers to Shanghai. According to yesterday's news, the Xinfeng had departed from Zhifu for Dalian yesterday afternoon and would be able to load the rescued crew members and passengers last night and sail to Shanghai. It is expected to arrive in Shanghai at the Jinliyuan Wharf at around 3 PM tomorrow. The bureau has appointed a special commissioner to take care of everything at the wharf together with the Junan Association.

Already Loaded on Tianjin Maru 106

Xinsheng News Agency reported that the China Merchants Bureau telegraphed its Tianjin and Yantai branches and the Xinfeng ship the day before yesterday, ordering them to quickly sail to Dalian to transfer the rescued crew members and passengers to Shanghai. At the same time, it telegraphed the Dalian agency to find a way to quickly transfer the rescued crew members and passengers to Shanghai by ship. Yesterday morning, it received a telegram from the Yantai branch that the Xinfeng ship had departed from Yantai for Dalian on the 13th and would no longer sail to Weihaiwei and would sail directly to Shanghai. It also received a telegram from the Dalian agency that the Tianjin Maru of the Dalian Steamship Company refused to transfer the rescued crew members and passengers. At 4 PM, another telegram was received stating that after the agency sent someone to negotiate, it was decided that the Tianjin Maru would transfer them and had departed from Dalian at noon on the 13th. It needs to sail to Qingdao and then to Shanghai. It takes twelve hours from Dalian to Qingdao, eight hours in Qingdao, and twenty-eight hours from Qingdao to Shanghai. It is expected to arrive in Shanghai tomorrow afternoon, and at the latest tomorrow morning. All fifty-three crew members will come to Shanghai, but only a few of the thirty-six passengers have returned to Yantai and Yingkou from Dalian. As for the Xinfeng ship, it will still sail to Dalian.

Liu and Deng's Telegram Reply to the Abolish War Association 107

Equally Criticizing Liu Wenhui

The headquarters of the Abolish Civil War Alliance has recently received the following telegrams from Liu Xiang and Deng Xihou:

Liu Xiang's Reply Telegram 108

To the Anti-War Grand Alliance and All Newspapers: Red bandits have invaded Sichuan, and Cangxi and Langzhong are successively reporting emergencies. I, Xiang, have repeatedly received clear orders from the Central Government to devise plans to suppress the bandits. Both local sentiment and my official duty do not allow for delay. Unfortunately, the war between Liu and Deng has broken out. At this time, despite repeated explanations, it is difficult to resolve the conflict. It is no secret that Sichuan province has become accustomed to regional separatism. Even in peacetime, there is strict mutual defense, and once war breaks out, all sides become even more entangled. I, Xiang, need to organize all the armies and assign tasks to comprehensively suppress the bandits. However, those at war are fighting on their own, not listening to any orders to stop. Those not yet at war are also being held back by these entanglements, causing worry and doubt to arise. This allows the red bandits to burn and destroy more each day. Who is obstructing us? It pains me to say. I have investigated that when the red bandits initially fled, they only captured Tongnan. Tian's army attacked with force and soon recovered it. However, because the war in western Sichuan broke out, Tian's army withdrew part of its forces for defense, allowing the embers of the defeated bandits to reignite their fierce flames. Moreover, Liu Wenhui took advantage of the fact that Xiang and Li Qixiang's troops were mobilizing to suppress the bandits, moving his troops to the west to pressure Rong Jian and to the east to threaten Liang Zi. On one hand, he continued to release water from the dams against Deng's army, constantly attacking, while falsely offering peace and ignoring loyal advice. Now that the internal strife has not stopped, the two armies themselves cannot undertake the bandit suppression work. Tian's troops are even more lacking in pay and provisions, exhausted from supporting the effort. The various departments are divided in their efforts, looking before and after. With such scattered troops encountering cunning and notorious communist bandits, a single unsuccessful attack will inevitably lead to further devastation. Moreover, Wenhui's constant internal strife, like draining a pond to catch fish or scattering seeds to drive away sparrows, has led to the hoisting of red flags and calls to resist taxation in various counties such as Qionglai, Pujiang, Mingshan, and Dayi in southern Sichuan. The red flames in northern Sichuan are blazing, and the surging waves in southern Sichuan are rising again. The red tide threatens to wash over the entire Sichuan, a truly terrifying prospect. I, Xiang, have both public and private feelings for Wenhui and sincerely hope that he will return from his wayward path and not stray too far. Therefore, even though I have been subjected to criticism from all sides, I have endured it. However, as the bandit threat increases daily and he continues on his misguided path, with both superiors and inferiors placing blame, I, Xiang, to stop the internal strife and cooperate in suppressing the communists, besides using a large portion of funds to subsidize the armies of Tian Songyao, Liu Jizhi, and Yang Zihui to defend against and suppress the red bandits and to contain their incursions, will also send a portion of troops westward to stop the internal strife. I hope that within a short period of time, obstacles can be removed so that we can pool our strength and cooperate together. This will allow us to comprehensively plan the overall situation, so that our strength is not divided, and we can be confident in suppressing the communists. Otherwise, the various armies will not be able to resolve their concerns, and the bandit suppression efforts will be difficult to be thorough. While it may seem urgent on the outside, it will actually be delayed, and any changes along the way will inevitably lead to major mistakes. It is my duty to defend our homeland and protect our fellow villagers. Compelled by righteousness, I will not complain of labor or resentment. Only when the red bandits are not eliminated and the people's suffering awaits relief, I, Xiang, for the sake of suppressing the red bandits and securing Sichuan, must simultaneously remove obstacles. I sincerely fear that various parties will not understand, and doubts and slanders will arise. Furthermore, those who create chaos will spread rumors, distorting the facts, confusing public opinion, and taking the opportunity for private gain, making right and wrong unclear and burying public justice. Therefore, I have briefly stated the general situation. I earnestly hope that you will carefully consider the situation in Sichuan, advocate for righteousness, and hope that the future of Sichuan depends on victory. I am filled with anticipation. This is my telegram to inform you, Liu Xiang bows, Geng.

Deng Xihou's Telegram 109

To the Anti-War Alliance: I received your telegram, earnestly advising and encouraging me to suppress the red bandits and cease hostilities. How dare I disobey? This time, Liu Wenhui has provoked trouble without cause, attacking our army, disregarding the national crisis, and showing no regard for the lives of the people. It has been two months since this began. I have sent repeated telegrams clearly stating the situation, hoping that you will understand. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has repeatedly telegraphed Wenhui to quickly return to his original defenses and not to act without authorization. Premier Wang also sent a telegram on June 6th, ordering him to cease hostilities and return to his defenses. The Alliance and the Sichuanese comrades have also sent letters and telegrams to advise and guide him, but Wenhui has ignored them all. To this day, he continues to attack without stopping, showing no remorse for the disaster he has caused, and hindering the suppression of the bandits. The facts are all there and cannot be concealed. His disregard for the Central Government and his obstinate and chaotic heart are extremely obvious. The Alliance deeply loves peace and upholds justice. I earnestly request that you forward the situation of Wenhui starting chaos and causing disaster in Sichuan, as well as his reckless militarism, to the Central Government. He should be punished appropriately and denounced to the people of the nation to warn those who engage in internal wars. This will clarify right and wrong and uphold public justice, so that the Sichuan situation can be settled quickly, allowing Supervisor Liu Xiang to coordinate the suppression of the bandits and provide peace to the common people. I cannot express my anticipation enough. Deng Xihou bows, Seal.
