Silk Factory Strike in the Concession Area Resolved This Morning 111

Shuang Gong Factory Also Strikes, Demanding Wage Increase

Single Palace Factories Have Agreed to Issue Supplementary Wages to Workers

After the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs persuaded workers in local silk factories to restore their treatment, a misunderstanding arose at the Jiyu Factory in the Zhabei district the day before yesterday over bonuses and wages, leading to a strike. After persuasion by the labor union, work resumed uniformly this morning. Five factories including the Xiangyuan factory in the concession area went on strike this morning due to wage deductions by the factory. After persuasion by the Social Affairs Bureau, the factories have agreed to issue supplementary wages and have scheduled to resume work this morning. Workers at the Shuang Gong Silk Factory also went on strike this morning, demanding a wage increase. Details are noted below:

Resumption of Work in Zhabei 112

Nineteen factories in the Zhabei district, including Yuanfengyong, Meifeng, and Fuyuan on Hengfeng Road; Wuxing on Meiyuan Road; Hongchun and Jiatai on Guangfu Road; Jiyu on Gonghe Road; Yuanji and Yuanxing on Yutong Road; and Baotai, Hongsheng, Xiexin, Yuanxin, Chuxin, Maofeng, Qianyuan, Shengtai, Zhenxing, and Jiyu Xiexin on Changan Road, were incited to strike due to Sunday bonuses and wage issues the day before yesterday. The Jiyu workers initiated the strike, which then spread to other factories, totaling 19. The fourth district and second sub-district of the Public Security Bureau was informed, and immediately dispatched police to maintain order. Wu Suzhen, the director of the sixth district silk reeling union, explained the situation to the workers, and the Social Affairs Bureau also sent Zhu Jintao to the Public Security Bureau to persuade the workers. It was decided to handle the matter in accordance with the mediation records signed a few days ago. As a result, all the female workers in the 19 factories resumed work this morning.

Spreading to the Concession 113

Five factories in the concession area, including Xiangyuan on Gansu Road, Yuyuan Yuji on Guoqing Road, and Yuanhe Taixin Jingwei on Alabaishi Road, implemented the wage restoration method determined by the Social Affairs Bureau's mediation decision, effective from June. However, the factories violated the decision, and the June wages were still issued at 45 cents. As a result, the Taixin workers initiated the strike, which then spread to the four factories of Yuyuan Yuji, Xiangyuan Jingwei, and Yuanhe. Fortunately, Yihe on North Chengdu Road and Xinchang in Caojiadu were not affected due to their distance. After the Social Affairs Bureau reported, Zhu Jintao was dispatched to persuade them and negotiate with the factory owners. At the same time, Yang Shumei, the director of the third district silk reeling union, explained the situation to the workers separately.

Supplementary Wages 114

After the workers in the concession area silk factories went on strike, they convened a meeting at the office of the Concession Silk Factory Association at 10:00 AM yesterday to discuss solutions. Jin Yusong of Xiangyuan, Wu Shengsan of Yuanhe, and Qiu Zhongchun of Yuyuan attended. Yang Shumei, the director of the third district silk reeling union, was also present. It was decided that factories that had already issued 45 cents would issue supplementary wages from the 16th of this month, in accordance with the mediation records of the Social Affairs Bureau's Mediation Committee. In the afternoon, the labor union persuaded the workers again, and the workers agreed to resume work at the factories this morning. In addition, the silk factories in the Zhabei district sent a letter to the Silk Factory Association yesterday, inquiring about the method of issuing wages to female workers in June. The Silk Factory Association replied that it should be implemented from June in accordance with the mediation decision.

Shuang Gong Strike 115

More than 400 workers at the Fulun Heng Shuang Gong Silk Factory at the end of Tianbao Road in Hongkou went on strike because the single palace factories in the Hongkou and Zhabei districts increased wages this time, while the Shuang Gong factory did not follow suit. This morning, when the factory opened, only two-tenths of the workers went to work, while the rest went on strike and sent representatives to the factory comprador, Shen Zubei, to demand that wages be issued in accordance with the wage distribution of the single palace factories as mediated by the Social Affairs Bureau this time. However, the factory manager said that according to past practice, the wages of the double palace were calculated at 80% of the single palace price. After the January 28th Incident, only Fulun was operating in the city. In order to take care of the interests of both parties, it was changed to 42 cents. Later, as the single palace factories gradually resumed operations, and in view of the sluggish silk market, the result of the meeting was that the wages were uniformly 42 cents. At that time, the double palace factory did not discount the price. Later, the single palace factory increased wages to 45 cents, and the double palace factory increased by one cent. The difference was minimal at this time, but the workers did not understand and demanded a wage increase. Therefore, the factory rejected the workers' demands. According to the factory manager Shen Zubei, who spoke to a reporter from New Sound News, the raw materials for the double palace are supplied by the single palace factory, so there are no benefits to be gained. Given the economic depression in society, if the factory were to close, no one would rent the factory site. At the same time, the factory takes into consideration the employees and workers, who would not have enough food and clothing if they lost their jobs. For this reason, the factory is doing its best to maintain operations, but it is often difficult to make ends meet. The workers are so unappreciative. In this situation, the factory has no choice but to close down and apologize to the workers.

Naming Ceremony of the Tianchu Aircraft, Aviation School Sends Aircraft to Participate in Performance 116

Aviation School Principal Mao Bangchu Sends Two Aircraft to Shanghai

The Significance of Choosing Hongqiao Airport as the Naming Location

It Is Possible to Commemorate the Relics of the Shanghai War and the Tomb of Short

Wu Yun Chu, the owner of Tianchu Monosodium Glutamate Factory, donated combat aircraft. The Junkers-style Tianchu aircraft has been assembled and is scheduled to hold a naming ceremony at Hongqiao Airport at 3:00 PM on the 16th. At that time, two Junkers-style aircraft from the Hangzhou Aviation School will come to Shanghai to perform technical demonstrations with the aircraft. The preparations are as follows:

Preparing the Ceremony 117

The Shanghai Aviation Association, together with the Tianchu Factory, negotiated the location for the naming ceremony and decided to hold it at Hongqiao Airport. From yesterday, the Tianchu Factory has been rushing to build colorful tents inside and outside the airport, and building a rostrum to prepare for the ceremony. They are also rushing to print order forms and admission tickets, which will be printed today and distributed to all sectors of society to invite them to visit.

Government Agency 118

The Assembled Tianchu Aircraft (Photo by Zhonghua Photo Studio)

Negotiating Location 119

The Tianchu aircraft was originally intended to be named in Jiangwan Racecourse, following the example of the Shanghai No. 1 aircraft naming ceremony. However, after consultation with the Aviation Administration and the Aviation Association, it was believed that Jiangwan Racecourse was not suitable for multiple aircraft to take off and land. At the same time, Hongqiao Airport was severely bombed by Japanese aircraft during the January 28th Incident, and there is also the tomb of the American righteous man Short, who helped us resist Japan. Usually, due to military relations, it is not open to the public. It is better to take this opportunity to allow people from all walks of life to enter and visit freely. In addition to watching the naming and performance of the Tianchu aircraft, they can also commemorate the bombed relics and the tomb of the American righteous man Short. Therefore, it was finally decided to hold the ceremony at Hongqiao Airport.

Venue Layout 120

Hongqiao Airport originally did not have stands and seating facilities. The Preparatory Office specially built them at the airport. Those holding tickets can enter the venue through the cordon. Those with invitations from the Aviation Association and Tianchu Monosodium Glutamate Factory can enter the special seats with their invitations. In addition, because the weather is hot, Guanshengyuan will sell cold drinks at the venue. Also, because the airport is far from the downtown area, although there are public buses back and forth, the number of buses is too small. There will definitely be many people attending on that day. A letter has been sent to the Public Works Bureau to inform the public bus company in the area to increase the number of buses or add special buses to facilitate transportation.

The Founding of the Jilin Volunteer Army Federation 129

The Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association received a report from the Jilin Province Volunteer Army Federation stating that after Su, Ma, Li, and Wang were forced to leave the country, all their subordinates remained hidden and ready to move. In addition, the small volunteer armies in various places coordinated with each other and repeatedly made meritorious contributions. Wherever their banners pointed, the Japanese were terrified. Among the lost provinces of Northeast China, there is still a ray of light, and that is the volunteer army that still exists. However, due to strong oppression, disrupted communications, distant mountains and rivers, and difficult journeys, it has been difficult to receive domestic assistance. Although representatives of various departments have appealed, assistance is still difficult to give and receive. Now, the volunteer armies of various departments have united to organize an agency to receive assistance from all parties. This is the reason for the organization of this association. The Northeast Volunteer Army has fought thousands of miles, bathed in blood for more than a year, without food or ammunition, but they still raise their arms and shout, and fight hard against the invaders. Wherever righteousness lies, they do not hesitate to sacrifice their lives. Regardless of the success or failure of their efforts, their sincere heart is commendable. If they receive sufficient assistance, they will be able to maneuver between the White Mountains and the Black Waters. How can the people of the whole country sit idly by? Recovering sovereignty and recovering lost territory is a shared responsibility, and there is no distinction between Qin and Yue. The purpose of the organization of this association is purely to receive assistance from all parties, and it does not contain any political or ideological activities, nor does it expand propaganda or sensationalize rumors. It only wants to receive assistance so that the Northeast Volunteer Army can extend its life and resistance. The Support Association is the active agency for assisting the Volunteer Army, and it has the obligation to support and assist this association. Therefore, we hereby request that you provide economic or material assistance. A declaration is attached, which mainly says that they will resist the enemy's artillery fire with their flesh and blood, and would rather be patriotic ghosts than slaves of a lost country. This ambition and this heart are pitiful and worthy of sympathy. It also describes that although the leaders Ma and Li have left the country, their subordinates still exist. Chen Zongdai, in the name of the Fourth Route Commander, took over as the commander of the Allied Forces, accommodated the remaining troops, and launched repeated counterattacks, breaking Mishan, capturing Fujin, and encircling Yilan. The facts are all there, and the merits are obvious. However, according to the person in charge of the Support Association, the association's donations to the Jilin Volunteer Army are all distributed and handled by the Jilin Volunteer Army Headquarters. Now that this document has been received, the organization members of the federation are being investigated.

Foreign Reports Explain Three-Month Grace Period for New Tax Rates 132

The Greater Shanghai Evening Post said that the customs authorities have agreed to the request of Chinese and foreign merchants and issued a notice that goods subject to tax that are withdrawn within three months from the date of implementation of the new tax on May 22 this year will still be taxed according to the old tax regulations promulgated in the 20th year of the Republic of China. Those who have already paid according to the new tax regulations can apply for a refund of the overpaid tax. According to the original customs regulations, this type of goods would be taxed according to the new tax regulations from the date of implementation of the new tax. Subsequently, the American Chamber of Commerce, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and other groups protested one after another. The authorities, taking into account the difficulties of the merchants, agreed to extend the grace period by three months.

Shanghai Telephone Bureau Decides to Automatically Cancel Chinese-Foreign Call Fee 136

Ministry of Communications Consults Municipal Government for Assistance

In Shanghai, there is a call fee of five cents for each Chinese rental telephone call. This fee is not only cumbersome but also very inconvenient for users. In order to facilitate Chinese rental telephone users, the Ministry of Communications specially ordered the Shanghai Telephone Bureau to consult with the Shanghai Telephone Company to cancel this call fee. However, the Shanghai Telephone Company said that there are tens of thousands of users in the concession and only thousands of Chinese telephone users in the Chinese area. If this call fee is cancelled, Chinese rental telephone calls will inevitably increase, and all the switchboards will not be sufficient. Therefore, they refused to cancel the fee. Although the Shanghai Telephone Bureau negotiated with the company several times, there was still no result. Now, the Shanghai Telephone Bureau believes that the Shanghai Telephone Company has no sincerity in cooperation, and the bureau has decided to take the initiative to cancel the fee to benefit users within the Chinese district. Once a reply is received, they will immediately start the process. The Ministry of Communications has also consulted the Municipal Government to instruct the Public Utilities Bureau to assist the Shanghai Telephone Bureau in carrying out the negotiations in order to realize the cancellation.

Urging Expedited Repair of the North Stone Cave Embankment 137

Yan Fenglou and others submitted to Chairman Gu, stating: Respectfully to Gu Jun, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, it is regarding the 125 zhang of the North Stone Cave Wild Goose Wing North Head Embankment in the Fifth District of Baoshan County. In September and October of last year, we telegraphed requesting the dispatch of personnel for surveying and estimating, and the allocation of funds for repair. We received Approval No. 1928 from your office, stating that the Construction Department had been instructed to handle the matter. Furthermore, we examined the Shen Xin and other newspapers dated October 29th, which recorded that the Baoshan North Stone Cave Wild Goose Wing North Head perilous construction expense was decided by your office in a meeting on the 28th, to be the responsibility of the Construction Department to order relevant counties to recognize and raise funds. Fenglou and others were deeply gratified upon receiving this good news. However, the project is extensive and requires significant funds. It may not be easy for the counties to raise the funds on time. Moreover, in late March, strong winds have been blowing continuously, causing severe damage and creating perilous situations, with the risk of collapse at any moment. Therefore, in April, on an auspicious day, we telegraphed your office again, requesting the swift allocation of funds for early repairs to avoid accidents. Subsequently, we received notification from the county government, relaying your instruction that the project would still await the determination of the funding method by the counties before comprehensive planning and repairs could be undertaken. We respectfully observe that this section of the embankment is adjacent to North Stone Cave and is located in a crucial area. During northeast winds, the water currents are even more turbulent. As with the repairs that were hastily carried out twenty years ago, the sparse reeds were washed away by the huge waves. Continuing the repairs last year, recent rains have caused the burlap sacks to rot, the soil to collapse, and the embankment surface to crumble, making it precarious. If urgent repairs are not undertaken, the autumn floods and high tides will soon arrive, making it impossible to defend against them. Fenglou and others have witnessed this situation and are extremely alarmed. Therefore, we are making our fifth appeal, humbly beseeching your office to promptly instruct the Construction Department to dispatch personnel for surveying and estimation, and at the same time, instruct the Finance Department to use the counties' old debts and urgent grain transport levies to raise significant funds from the banking sector within a set timeframe for completion. Otherwise, not only will the entire county's population be buried in the fishes' bellies, but the fields, houses, and lives of people in nearby counties will also be affected. The local people have fulfilled their tax obligations and should have the right to protection of life and property. We are telegraphing again with utmost urgency, imploring you to approve and implement this promptly. We await your instructions with utmost anxiety. Respectfully submitted by Yan Fenglou, Township Head of Huiyuan Township in the Fifth District of Baoshan County, Li Fengming, Deputy Township Head, and all the Township Residents.

Machine Federation Requests Exemption from Double Taxation on Silk and Cotton Interwoven Fabrics 138

The Shanghai Machine Federation submitted a document to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, stating: Regarding cotton and silk interwoven fabrics, customs duties are duplicated, and domestically produced cloths are unable to bear the burden. We are submitting this request for exemption based on the distressed situation of Suzhou merchants. The Sanxin, Mingxin, and other dyeing and weaving factories have informed the federation that, with the exception of pure cotton yarn woven products, for which the cotton yarn tax payment certificate can be used to offset the export certificate, cotton and rayon interwoven fabrics cannot be used to offset and must still be assessed and pay a 7.5% export tariff. Those without a label must be assessed and charged 12.5%. If transported to non-unified tax areas, another export tax must be levied. Moreover, the rayon portion included in the interwoven fabrics has already paid a high luxury import tax of 80%. In addition, there are various harsh taxes and levies in the provinces, such as the landing tax in Sichuan and the production and sales tax in Jiangxi (i.e., bandit suppression and rehabilitation donation). Investigations reveal that the amount of rayon in interwoven fabrics only accounts for 1% to 20% of the total weight, never exceeding 20%, while cotton yarn that has already paid the unified tax accounts for 80% to 99%. However, the customs duty burden is as mentioned above, a duplication. On the other hand, foreign goods imported into our country, whether they are pure cotton woven products, or interwoven fabrics of cotton and wool, cotton and silk, or cotton, hemp, wool, and silk, only pay one import tax, and when re-exported, they can be transported without hindrance with a pass and are exempt from double taxation. The preferential treatment is such that our domestic goods, when transported and sold within the country, face difficulties and setbacks. The disparity is obvious, and the unfairness is extreme. We investigate that foreign goods are able to dump in our country's market, implementing its economic aggression, because of the inequality of our country's tariff and armed with its strong capital, excellent technology, catering to the consumer's psychology, strangling our fate. If we do not rise up to protect and promote, how can our machine-made domestic woven fabrics of interwoven cotton survive and compete with foreign goods? Inevitably, they will follow in the footsteps of native cloth, being defeated one by one. The federation, in view of the precariousness of domestic industry, is on the verge of bankruptcy, and the cotton weaving industry is particularly severe. We humbly request the government to sympathize with the difficulties of merchants, adhere to the principle of one item, one tax, protect domestic goods, encourage domestic production, immediately exempt interwoven fabrics from re-export tax, increase the import tax on rayon and various woven fabrics, in order to counter and seek survival. It is a vital move to revitalize our country's industry. Therefore, we are submitting this request based on the facts, humbly requesting your ministry to review and approve the request, (transfer to the Ministry of Finance) order the customs to exempt, in order to relieve the difficulties of Suzhou merchants and benefit domestic goods. We await your instructions with utmost anxiety. Respectfully submitted to the National Government Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry (Approved by the Ministry of Industry and transferred to the Ministry of Finance for review).

Serious Labor Dispute at Electric Company, Labor Side Presented Four Demands Yesterday 141

Yuan Ludeng to Mediate Today

Appeals Committee Issues Appeal to All Sectors

Workers at the Yangshupu New Factory of the Shanghai Electric Company recently had a dispute over the demand for severance pay for foreman Yang Aqiao, and the company further dismissed union directors Ni Wenfu, Chen Baogen, Pan Genlin, etc., on the 5th of this month, leading to a sudden escalation of the labor dispute. After the union convened a meeting of old and new factory foremen, it was resolved to present four proposals for improving treatment to the company and demand the reinstatement of the dismissed workers. If there is no result, a full-force confrontation will be determined. Mr. Yuan Ludeng, a Chinese director, will visit company Vice President Heert this afternoon to mediate. The details are recorded below.

Letter to the General Manager 142

The Water and Electricity Union of the Fourth District yesterday presented four treatment proposals and requested the reinstatement of dismissed workers, in a letter to the company's general manager, stating: Esteemed General Manager, With utmost respect, Your company dismissed Ni Wenfu, Chen Baogen, Pan Genlin, Zhang Caisheng, and others on the 7th of this month without any reason. All the workers and foremen of the two factories were deeply surprised upon hearing this. An investigation reveals that Ni Wenfu and the other four individuals are of upright character and diligent in their work. It seems unnecessary to dismiss them. Moreover, when the Shanghai Municipal Council Electricity Department was transferred to your company in April 1929, Mr. Mou Fei, the Shanghai representative of the American and Foreign Company, solemnly declared that the jobs of workers would be protected, as secure as they were under the Shanghai Municipal Council. Even in the middle of last year, you, sir, repeatedly declared to the workers that they would not be dismissed without reason. The words are still ringing in our ears. We believe that you, sir, will certainly not forget them. However, now you are doing the opposite. We believe that this measure is extremely inappropriate. Now, the workers and foremen of both factories are uneasy about this situation. After repeated meetings, we believe that if Ni Wenfu and the other four cannot be reinstated, then all the workers and foremen will not be able to work with peace of mind, and a state of terror will be created. Therefore, we are taking the liberty of submitting this letter of request, immediately withdrawing the dismissal order to calm the public, and attaching four proposals for improving worker treatment. We sincerely hope that you will review and implement them. It would be our greatest fortune. We have scheduled Liu Linsheng, Wang Xingen, Yang Zhaogen, Zhang Lianhai, and others to pay you a visit on the 13th of this month. We hope that you will grant us an audience at that time and reply as soon as possible. With utmost impatience, we await your instructions. Respectfully submitted by all the workers and foremen of the two factories of the Shanghai Electric Company.

Four Conditions 143

The detailed contents of the four proposals for improving worker treatment are as follows: (1) Pension and Severance Pay: When workers retire, the company should pay a 5% pension. If workers are laid off due to a factory slowdown, in addition to the above pension, they should be given severance pay equal to three months' wages. The aforementioned pension is compensation for the workers' years of hard work and is not a large amount at 5%. As for the severance pay, due to the current economic downturn and the large number of unemployed people, it is difficult to find work once retired. Therefore, we ask the company to sympathize with the workers' hard work and distress and issue additional severance pay to avoid affecting their livelihood. (2) Sick Leave and Medical Expenses: Workers' wages during sick leave should be paid at the original rate. If patients are hospitalized for treatment, all expenses should be borne by the company. Workers' monthly wages are very meager, barely enough to make a living, with no savings. Shorting one day's wages is shorting one day's food. Therefore, wages during sick leave should be paid as usual, and hospital expenses should also be borne to avoid increasing the workers' burden due to illness. (3) Compensation for Injuries and Deaths: Workers who die or become disabled due to work should be compensated generously. The compensation method is as follows: For those who have adult children, compensation of 2,000 yuan. If the children are young, compensation should be given according to the Zhou Genfa case. If there are many young children, the amount of compensation should be increased proportionally based on the Zhou Genfa case. If disabled due to work, the original salary should be paid until old age. (4) Annual Bonus: All those who have worked in the factory for one full year should be given an annual bonus equal to one month's wages at the end of each year as a reward. This annual bonus has been referenced to the treatment of workers in various factories, and it is generally the case, not an excessive request.

Yuan to Mediate Today 144

Since the escalation of the dispute, the Shanghai General Labor Union, in order to seek a swift resolution, dispatched Executive Committee member Shao Xubai yesterday morning, accompanied by union representatives Ni Wenfu, Pan Genlin, Yang Zhaogen, Zhang Caisheng, and others, to meet with Chinese director Yuan Ludeng at No. 1 Bund, Avenue Edward VII, to request him to mediate. Mr. Yuan expressed his willingness to be responsible for mediating and hoped that the workers would wait patiently for a solution. It is reported that Mr. Yuan has scheduled to visit Heert at the company's headquarters on Sazhi Road at 2:00 PM today to mediate.

Appeal to All Sectors 145

The union's appeals committee issued an appeal to all sectors yesterday, stating: Fellow countrymen of all sectors across the country, public concession water and electricity users, in the present scientific age, production relies on machinery and electricity, which is the driving force of social production and an indispensable thing for the city. In the past, the Shanghai Municipal Council Electricity Department was sold for 85 million taels to the Shanghai Electric Company. In order to protect the interests of users and Chinese employees, the Shanghai Municipal Council stipulated with the company that accepted the Electricity Department that electricity prices should not be increased arbitrarily, employees should not be laid off arbitrarily, and efforts should be made to develop the electricity business forward, complete a complete electrical construction, reduce electricity prices, improve employee treatment, and effectively protect the existing treatment of employees, and deposit one million taels in the current company as the Shanghai Municipal Council's employee pension. Now, the Shanghai Electric Company, for the sake of profit, relying on the power of imperialism, violates the articles of association, and with the qualification of a monopoly business in the public concession, arbitrarily raises prices. It has increased electricity prices twice in less than four years. It treats our employees by dismissing them in large numbers, swallowing pensions, using low-paid new workers, dismissing old workers, destroying worker organizations, dismissing union directors without reason, deducting pensions on false pretenses, and is unwilling to accept the mediation of our country's government agencies. Fellow countrymen, the imperialists are so fierce. For their own interests, our two thousand employees have no choice but to fight against the imperialist capitalists. For the interests of the entire nation, they have no choice but to resist the imperialists. They are still in a state of mutual hostility. We hope that all sectors will speak out for justice and provide sympathetic assistance. We hereby declare.

Dazhong Rubber Factory Paid Severance Pay Yesterday Afternoon 147

Regarding the case of the stoppage of the dispute at the Dazhong Rubber Factory on Xinjia Slope Road, Shanghai West, the Social Affairs Bureau decided to resolve it. All workers were allowed to be dismissed, and the factory paid each person a severance pay of 20 yuan, half of which was paid first. The remainder would be paid after two months if work had not resumed, or if work resumed, it would be waived. However, the workers demanded a one-time payment, which the employers did not agree to. Therefore, when the employers distributed the payment at the Social Affairs Bureau the day before yesterday, the workers were unwilling to receive it. Fortunately, after explanation by the Social Affairs Bureau mediation director Wang Xianqing and persuasion by the Jin section chief of the third section of the first district of the Public Security Bureau, they dispersed. At 1:00 PM yesterday, they returned to Yaowang Temple in the Nanshi area, where the employers paid half of the amount, 10 yuan per person, in accordance with the mediation record. The Social Affairs Bureau sent Li Guilin to supervise, and the Public Security Bureau sent police to protect. As a result, the workers all received the payment. A total of 116 people were paid. Those who have not received the payment will continue to be paid at the factory starting today.

Social Affairs Bureau Orders Insurance Industry to List Insurance Documents in Both Chinese and Foreign Languages 149

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, after the proposal of the Shoe Leather Nail Industry Association and others at the Fourth Member Representative Assembly that insurance documents should uniformly abolish foreign languages and use Chinese, resolved to amend and submit it to the Social Affairs Bureau for review. Now, the approval states: Received and acknowledged. This case was previously submitted by this bureau to the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce for instructions and interpretation. International practice stipulates that the language to be used in commercial contracts has no fixed rules and should be determined according to commercial customs in various regions. As for foreign insurance companies, on the grounds of business relations, even if there are places where foreign languages need to be used on the documents, at least Chinese and foreign languages must be listed in parallel to prevent merchants from being deceived and to achieve the purpose of regaining sovereignty. As for insurance companies and policyholders that are both Chinese, they should respect the national system and facilitate the majority of policyholders. Even if market customs or other factors require the use of foreign languages, both Chinese and foreign languages must be listed in parallel, with Chinese as the main language. This bureau has ordered the Shanghai Insurance Industry Association to comply with these requirements. In view of the above, in addition to ordering the Insurance Association to correct this as soon as possible, you are hereby notified of this approval.

International Trade Bureau Releases the Current Commercial Situation of Overseas Chinese in Fiji 151

Operating in Rice, Sugar, Ramie, Coconut, and Timber as the Basis

All Industries Are Depressed Due to the Impact of the Economic Downturn

The Guidance Department of the International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry yesterday released the current business situation of overseas Chinese native product merchants in Fiji. The original text reads: Fiji's native products mainly include rice, sugar, ramie, coconut, tobacco, and timber. Most of the overseas Chinese engaged in business here use these native products as the basis. In recent years, they have been severely depressed due to the impact of the economic downturn, and the situation last year was even worse than before. The general situation of the overseas Chinese native product merchants in the past year is described below:

Rice Market Stable 152

Overseas Chinese control 80% of Fiji's rice industry, with strong power. During the heyday, they had the power to control the market. Today, however, times have changed greatly. In recent years, native products have fallen in price, and the Fijian economy has experienced panic. As a result, many people have improved maize and the like, and rice sales have been greatly affected. The value of those exported overseas is only more than 30,000 Fijian dollars, which is almost twice as different from the 80,000 Fijian dollars of the previous year. Fortunately, the market price was still stable last year (about 5 Fijian dollars per bag), and the overseas Chinese rice merchants suffered few losses.

Sugar Industry Depressed 153

In the past, overseas Chinese had a considerable part of the sugar industry in Fiji. In the past six or seven years, large-scale sugar factories established by Europeans, Americans, and Fijians have been established in many places, with new manufacturing methods and excellent product quality. Chinese merchants have been greatly affected. It is found that most of Fiji's sugar production is sold to the United States. Last year, 13 million dans of the total Fiji sugar production of about 14 million dans were sold to the United States. The Chinese merchants are engaged in domestic trade in Fiji and have no exports. In this time of economic panic, the Fijians' purchasing power has decreased, and the operation has been quite depressed.

Ramie Production Reduced 154

The quantity of Fiji ramie production used to increase year by year. In recent years, the price has fallen more and more, and farmers have found it unprofitable to plant, and production has gradually decreased. Last year, the best overseas market for ramie was Japan. Therefore, except for Japanese ramie merchants in Fiji who obtained considerable profits, the rest were unprofitable. Many overseas Chinese engaged in this industry have abandoned it due to losses in recent years. It will become more and more reduced in the future.

Coconut Merchants Suffer Losses 155

Last year, overseas Chinese coconut profits were unprofitable, as in the previous year. The reason is that the industry cannot cooperate. When they buy copra from farmers, they mutually increase the purchase price. The cost is already high, and they cannot wait for a good price to sell. As a result, some even suffered losses. The way to remedy this is to strive for cooperation.

Timber Declines 156

Overseas Chinese timber merchants in Fiji used to make a lot of profit, but now the golden age has passed, and they have even suffered losses. Last year's situation was the most declining in the past ten years. The reasons for the decline of the timber industry are nothing more than business competition, oversupply, and price decline. In the past six or seven years, the number of overseas Chinese timber yards has increased by more than 80 (now there are about 800 in total). Three years ago, when sales were broad, supply and demand were met, and business was booming, the profits were good. Today, however, foreign trade is almost cut off, and on the island itself, due to economic panic, construction has decreased, and sales are not as good as before. The most important remedy is to reduce production and meet supply and demand. There will be no competition, and prices will naturally rise.

Heavy Tobacco Tax Increase 157

Last year, operators in Fiji, whether foreign or Chinese merchants, were unprofitable. The reason is that exports of tobacco leaves have decreased. The Fiji government's heavy tobacco leaf tax is also an obstacle to development. The remedies are to expand the export tobacco leaf market and the Fiji government to increase the foreign cigarette population tax.

The Sichuan Merchant Guild Urges Relief for Refugees in Northern Sichuan 158

The Sichuan Merchant Guild, deeply concerned about the plight of tens of thousands of people in Northern Sichuan who have been displaced by war and banditry, rendered homeless and starving, has sent a letter to the Shanghai Jisheng Society, earnestly requesting the allocation of funds for relief efforts. The letter states: "Respected Sirs, our province's Northern Sichuan, including Baoning and the Jianzhong counties, has always been known for its poverty and hardship. In recent years, drought and the exploitation by stationed troops have made life unbearable for the people. However, due to its remote location, poor transportation, and a lack of talented individuals to handle affairs, the region has been unable to appeal for help from the outside world. As a result, the extreme suffering endured by the people, akin to living in hell, is little known to outsiders. This time, taking advantage of the internal conflicts among Sichuan warlords, the Red Bandits fled from Shaanxi into Sichuan. When they initially occupied counties such as Tongjiang, Nanjiang, and Bazhong, many refugees sought shelter within the city walls, placing an additional burden on the already strained local resources. After the exploitation by the stationed troops, the Red Bandits further extorted donations from the people under the pretext of suppressing banditry. Pitiful residents, already struggling to survive, were unable to cope. Consequently, some abandoned their fields and houses, fleeing in secret, while others resorted to suicide. Such tragic scenes are numerous. With no strength to suppress the bandits, the stationed troops retreated from the city of Lu in June 20, they even arbitrarily robbed the people, looting the city inside and out, leaving it completely empty. The people had long heard of the Red Bandits' cruel massacres wherever they went, and everyone was terrified. Therefore, when the retreating troops engaged in robbery, the people mistakenly believed that the Red Bandits were attacking. Consequently, both the young, the old, and those already displaced, only knew to flee for their lives, disregarding everything else. They fled together.

Coinciding with a major rise in the river water levels, the retreating troops had already seized the boats. In addition to the more than three thousand people who drowned while scrambling to cross the river, it is estimated that approximately fifty to sixty thousand men, women, and children fled to Shunqing, while another forty to fifty thousand fled to Tongchuan and Mianzhou. To this day, they live in makeshift shelters, without any assistance. Sichuan warlords are preoccupied with their internal power struggles and pay no attention to the refugees. Moreover, they suspect that the refugees are intermingled with Red Bandits and have prohibited them from traveling elsewhere, leaving them with no way out, without clothing or food. Without urgent assistance, they can only await their doom. This is the situation for those who managed to reach the towns and cities; countless others fled in disarray, lost their way, and wandered on the roads. Their dire circumstances defy description. Letters are pouring in from all directions, requesting us to appeal to charitable organizations and philanthropists in Shanghai to raise funds and remit them to Chongqing as quickly as possible, so that relief efforts can be carried out on the front lines. They emphasize that the sooner, the better, as any delay may be too late. Our guild, aware of the difficult times and the widespread disasters across the provinces, understands the limitations of your society's resources. However, aside from your esteemed society, to whom can we appeal? Furthermore, after investigation, we confirm that the situation in Jianzhong and other counties is indeed severe, mainly due to their remote location, poor transportation, and lack of outside awareness. We respectfully request that your esteemed society display great compassion and generously provide relief. Not only will the dying refugees be blessed, but the members of our guild will also be deeply grateful. We humbly submit this request, seeking the kind consideration of the charitable gentlemen of the Jisheng General Assembly. Respectfully submitted by the Sichuan Merchants' Public Welfare Association."

In the Kidnapping Case of Shen Mengyi, the Manager of the Inland River Merchants Bureau Is Also an Accomplice 160

丨Zhou Yinglong Was Extradited from Zhenjiang to Shanghai Yesterday丨

Shen Mengyi, a native of Huzhou, worked in the foreign exchange department of the Bank of China and was the son of Shen Tianxin. On the morning of the 20th of last month, at 8 a.m., he left home in car number 2085. After dropping off his sister, Yiyao, at the Customs Library on Xinzha Road, as he was about to return to the car to go to the Bank of China, a group of kidnappers suddenly seized Shen and demanded a large ransom. Subsequently, thanks to the efforts of Chief Detective You A'gen of the Zhabei Police Station, Detectives Liu Junqing and Zhou Guisen, and Detective Shen Jinwen, Shen was rescued at 559 Lafayette Road in the French Concession. The ringleaders of the kidnappers, Ma Qiaosheng and Ma Rongsheng, along with twenty others, were apprehended. Three pistols and sixteen bullets were confiscated. The First Special Court has since ordered them detained for interrogation. This matter has already been reported in this newspaper. Ma Qiaosheng has now confessed that Zhou Yinglong (also known as Zhou Younan), a native of Yangzhou, is also an accomplice in this case. Zhou currently serves as the manager of the Inland River Merchants Bureau in Zhenjiang. Detective You requested the First Special Court to issue an official document, instructing the detective to cooperate with the local Public Security Bureau on the 11th of this month and arrest Zhou in Room 38 of the Wuzhou Hotel at 2 Yingshan Street. Zhou was extradited to Shanghai yesterday and brought before the First Special Court's Criminal Division this morning. The police station's lawyer, Ru Baoyi, explained the previous circumstances and requested that Zhou Yinglong be tried together with Ma Qiaosheng and the others. Judge Qian Hongye approved the request and ordered Zhou Yinglong to be detained and tried together with Ma Qiaosheng and the others at a later date.

Dafeng to Undertake the Silver Dollar Transport on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Line 162

The transportation of silver dollars on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railways was previously handled separately by the Dafeng (Beijing-Shanghai Line) and Tonghe (Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Line) transportation companies. This month, the contract with the Tonghe Company expired, and the responsibility for transporting silver dollars on both Shanghai-Hangzhou lines has been consolidated under the Dafeng Company. This has been reported to the Ministry by the Railway Bureau and approved. However, the formal contract is still being drafted and has not yet been signed. Because the Tonghe Company is announcing its closure today, the Railway Bureau, to facilitate the transport of silver dollars, has approved the Dafeng Company to take over the responsibility immediately and bear full responsibility, in addition to quickly formalizing the contract.

Guangdong Warehouse Miscellaneous Grains are Moldy 164

The goods stored in the Taikoo warehouses in Guangdong, which have been monitored and prohibited from unloading by the Seamen's Union, are worth a total of six to seven million yuan. Taikoo also telegraphed Huang Yongxue, Chairman of the Guangdong Provincial Federation of Commerce, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, with the same telegram.

Labor Strike Moves to Shanghai for Negotiations 165

Taikoo Company believes that the current labor strike was provoked by the Guangdong Seamen's Union using the issue of the dismissal of the stewards on the Wusong Wheel as a pretext. The Wusong is a Yangtze River vessel and does not sail to Nanhua. Since the issue concerns the Yangtze River region, the negotiations should not take place in Guangdong. Even if both parties discuss the matter, it should not be negotiated in Guangdong. The company has already presented its views to the Shanghai General Seamen's Union, stating that it is difficult to resolve the issue in Guangdong, and that there is room for discussion if it is moved to the Shanghai General Union.

The Chen Baosheng Portion of the Xin Renhe Wheel Tragedy Concludes Interrogation 166

丨Sentence Scheduled for the 19th丨

The continued trial of Chen Baosheng, the assistant comprador in the Xin Renhe steamboat murder case involving five deaths, has been previously reported. Yesterday morning at 9 a.m., Judge Luo opened the court for debate. The official asked Chen Baosheng for his confession: "I only knew when I arrived at the dock." The official asked, "Where did you sign?" Chen replied, "On the ship. After it docked. I asked Wang Guanxian what had happened, and he said there were five pirates. One fell down himself, and four were pushed down by the passengers. They are dead. Then they told me to sign." At this point, Prosecutor Zhang Zi was asked to present his opinion, stating that the defendant had premeditated and incited the murder of Ma Koubao and others. The other defendants had all confessed that Chen Baosheng had told them to sign, and that he had discussed the matter with Sun Xingsheng and others beforehand, as Ye Yuanfu had explained in detail, "The gentlemen held a meeting, and Chen Baosheng was also present." Therefore, it is very clear. At this point, the defendant's lawyer, Li Mo, argued that, according to the facts, Chen Baosheng had already left the ship at Xingang to attend a wedding feast at Zhang Chengkang's house, and that it was only after Xingang that they reached Lingdian Port. Chen Baosheng was no longer present. Why should Chen Baosheng share the responsibility for others trying to cover up the crime? According to common psychology, the accused often attribute the blame to those who are not present to make themselves look better. Furthermore, signing is only a passive prevention of objections, not incitement or premeditation. Even conspiracy to commit murder is far-fetched. At this point, the lawyers for the victims, Yao Jiapeng and Tian Long, etc., each requested an ancillary civil lawsuit. The family member, Madam Ma Chen, shouted loudly in the court, "Their steamboat secretly smokes opium and premeditated murder. They sought wealth and killed. Robber ships! The murderers must pay with their lives! The company should pay compensation!" The judge said, "It will be handled according to the law." He then announced the end of the debate, set the sentencing for the 19th, and ordered the defendant to be returned to custody.

French National Day Celebrated Today 167

Today is the anniversary of the founding of the French Republic. The authorities of the French Concession in Shanghai, as well as officials, gentry, merchants, and scholars residing in Shanghai, will hold a grand celebration. The French Consul-General has instructed the French Municipal Council to prepare for all matters beforehand, as previously reported in this newspaper. All institutions will be closed today. The Avenue Joffre and Avenue Dubail area, all the way to the Gujiat宅 Garden, will be decorated with lanterns and colored lights along the streets. Crowds of people will stroll and throng the streets. The Chief Inspector of the French Police Department, fearing that criminals and petty thieves may mingle and cause trouble, has specifically ordered all police stations to dispatch additional Chinese, Western, and Vietnamese detectives to patrol in sections to maintain order. At 8:00 a.m. this morning, the commander of the French garrison in Shanghai, together with the French Consul-General, gathered French army and navy soldiers stationed in Shanghai at the original site of the New Bund Garden on Avenue Joffre to hold a military review ceremony. At 9:00 a.m., French Consul-General Meyrier led his colleagues and military and police officers to hold a flag-raising ceremony in front of the consulate. At noon, a celebration was held in the consulate's main hall, inviting officials, gentry, merchants, and scholars from various countries. In addition, the Third Special District Local Court suspended the hearing of minor cases due to the police department's holiday for National Day celebrations. However, self-prosecuted criminal cases and civil cases were heard as usual.

Public Concession Sanitary Condition 168

The Acting Director of the Shanghai Municipal Council Health Department's work report for June states that in terms of mortality rate, the month showed generally good health. The mortality rate for foreigners was 6.73 per thousand, a decrease of 2.11 from the previous month. This was due to fewer deaths from infectious diseases, and also due to a decrease in the number of deaths of Japanese residents. The number of deaths for Chinese was 1,048, with a rate of 11.81 per thousand. As for birth statistics, there were 74 foreigners and 158 Chinese reported, an increase from the previous month.

Infectious Diseases 169

The most severe disease among foreigners was gastroenteritis, tuberculosis, and dysentery. Regarding gastroenteritis, more attention should be paid to injections. The abundance of dysentery is related to the season. Among the Chinese, tuberculosis, gastroenteritis, diphtheria, scarlet fever, and dysentery were prevalent, with tuberculosis being particularly numerous. Inoculations against cholera were performed on 56,054 people this month. Two hundred people were vaccinated at various sanitary sub-offices.

Pathological Research 170

The pathological laboratory conducted 1,554 tests and manufactured over 100 liters of cholera injection serum. At the rabies treatment center, 78 people came seeking treatment, five of whom came from other cities to Shanghai for treatment. Sixty people were treated, including 19 who received prophylactic treatment and 25 who received full treatment. The remaining 16 had started but not completed their treatment, which is quite regrettable.

Veterinary Report 171

The average daily milk production this month was 3.68% lower than the previous month. Several samples of "A" grade milk were found to be unsatisfactory. Re-testing of a certain cattle herd one year later showed that the reaction rate increased from 64.3% to 83.4%. Three cattle died of contagious pneumonia, and nine died of other causes. Work at the slaughterhouses continued as usual. The number of pigs slaughtered was 9.1% less than the previous month, which is normal for the season.

Food Inspection 172

Business at the vegetable markets was quite good, and they were inspected and their weights and measures were corrected at any time. The Xiaoshadu Road vegetable market is about to be completed and opened for use. Bakeries are still inspected day and night, and are generally in good condition. Restaurants, taverns, etc., with licenses are repeatedly inspected to maintain sanitary standards. 201 applications for business licenses were investigated.

Sanitation Work 173

Special attention has been paid to fly and mosquito control. Ditches have been cleared and oiled. Mosquito larvae were found in the central district, which has not happened for many years. Therefore, the public is asked to cooperate with the Health Department. All broken bottles, broken jars, etc., that can collect water should not be discarded at will. The Gambusia fish farm on Jiaozhou Road currently has a large number of "Gambusia" fish. If private ponds need them, they can contact the Chief Sanitary Inspector (telephone 12410 extension 23) for a very low fee. The Public Works Department is also paying attention to fly control at the garbage dumps in the east and west districts. A portion of the East District shacks has been removed, and several unregistered and unsanitary shacks in the West District have been notified to relocate.

Summer Precautions 174

Care must be taken to prevent flies from contaminating food and drinks. Also, the summer sun reflects off the water and white walls, causing discomfort and even harming the eyes. Therefore, those going out are best to wear dark glasses with side mirrors to protect their eyesight. This is very important for those boating or traveling on the water.

Shangbao Tobacco and Alcohol License Still Follows the Old Rules 175

Conflict Has Ended

Since the Shangbao Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Office has been operated by Ding Xie this year, it has sought to double the collection amount. The city's tobacco and alcohol industries protested this as a group, and after repeated negotiations by representatives from various industry associations, the office agreed to follow the old rules. The industries were satisfied. However, the other day, Renxing on Xibaoxing Road in Zhabei and Dashengchang on Fangxie Road in Nanshi were instructed to bring their licenses to the office to pay taxes and exchange for new licenses, but the collection directors of the north and south offices detained them and demanded a donation of four yuan for a two-yuan license, almost causing a dispute. Fortunately, Teng Zhixiang and Tong Lingyun, directors of the Shanghai North Branch Office of the Tobacco Industry Association, personally went to the tax office to negotiate. Director Ding explained that it was a misunderstanding and promised to instruct the staff to handle the matter as usual and no longer harass them. The conflict then came to an end.

Unanimously Opposed the Construction of a Vegetable Market on the Railway Station Road

The merchants and vendors of Jiangyin Street in the Shanghai South District held a plenary representative joint meeting at around 2 p.m. yesterday, and publicly elected Zhang Mingchang as the temporary chairman. Send another letter to charitable organizations to relieve the suffering of the poor. 4. When necessary, all merchants and vendors will close their businesses. 5. When necessary, discuss concrete coping methods. 6. When necessary, issue a declaration detailing the harm of moving the Jiangyin Street vendors to the Railway Station Road and the danger that stores will close. After the discussion, the meeting was adjourned at 5:30 p.m.

A Record of Fundraising Through Opera Performance at the Pushan Villa 177

Held at the Tianchan Stage on the Evening of the 17th

The Pushan Villa specializes in charitable deeds such as burying the exposed, providing medical treatment, and giving medicine. It has been around for more than 20 years, relating public health, good very shallow fresh. During this summer, the weather is hot, and various seasonal epidemic hospitals are opened one after another. Whenever there is a sudden death or death on the road and others who are unable to collect and bury the body, the villa is responsible for providing coffins and burial, fulfilling its obligations to the fullest extent. This has long been known to the public. However, the villa has never had any funds, relying entirely on the generous donations of philanthropists from all walks of life to maintain its operations. Since the January 28th Incident, all industries have been in decline, and fundraising has been difficult. However, the work in progress has increased rather than decreased, and the cost of labor and materials has gradually become more expensive, creating a situation of great strain. Recently, we heard that celebrities in Shanghai and comrades from the Leshan Society initiated a fundraising opera performance at the Tianchan Stage on the night of the 17th of this month. Li Hengfeng will perform "Driving Three Passes," Chen Liangyu, Wang Jinmei, and Wang E'yan will perform "Returning to the Dragon Pavilion," Wang Shurong will perform "Taking the High Deng," Qian Juyou and Wang Shuying will perform "Empty City Stratagem," Peng Guohuan will perform "Picking a Carriage," Wang Shusheng will perform "Escorting Prisoners," Yao Mulian and Yao Jicai will perform "Original Mole," Du Jimei and Wang Jizhou will perform "Beaded Curtain Village," the two ladies Lu Guifang and Lu Guifen will perform "Four Pans Mountain," Wang Detian and Fan Hengde will perform "Ascending to Heaven," You Jusun will perform "Five Elders Meeting," Yuan Ludeng and Zheng Mengxia, Jiang Bogong will perform "Double Lion Picture," Dong Dangbin will perform "Three Iron Roosters" and other masterful works. With the enthusiastic support of the Actors' Association, actors such as Zhao Ruquan and Lin Shusen will participate and specially perform the treacherous play "Wagang Village." At that time, people from all walks of life will come together to support this charity event, and it will surely be a grand occasion.

The Silver Ear Mushroom Guild Opposes Increased Tax on Silver Ear Mushrooms 178

丨A Sudden Increase of Three Times the Original Tax Rate丨

Wanyuan County in Sichuan has always been a place that produces silver ear mushrooms. Because it is connected to Tongba, it has been disturbed by the Red Bandits, who have already occupied the Zhuyu Pass, Liujiaba, Sanxikou, Shuanglong Temple, and other places in the county. The county magistrate, using military affairs as a pretext, invited silver ear mushroom merchants to the county government and ordered them to pay an additional ten yuan per catty. Therefore, letters of distress have been pouring in. The merchants who have already purchased the mushrooms cannot deliver them to Shanghai and are still waiting for a solution. The local guild held an emergency meeting yesterday and unanimously decided to oppose the tax increase. It urgently telegraphed Superintendent Liu of Suiding, requesting him to order the cancellation of the tax increase and not to stop until the goal is achieved. The telegram reads as follows: "Superintendent Liu of Suiding, your Excellency: We were shocked to learn from numerous letters from our colleagues that the silver ear mushroom tax in Wanyuan, in addition to the original three yuan and two jiao per catty, has recently been forced to increase by ten yuan per catty. Silver ear mushroom producing areas mostly have customers who come to purchase them. A heavy tax will inevitably discourage them, leading to rural bankruptcy. Furthermore, there is a glut of supply in Shanghai, resulting in significant losses. If the county needs military funds, it would be better to make other plans. We humbly request that your Excellency immediately order the cancellation of the tax increase to alleviate the merchants' difficulties and maintain the local products. We also request a reply. Li Qingfan, Chairman of the Shanghai Silver Ear Mushroom Industry Association, respectfully."

Interrogation Record of Kidnapper of Wang Delin 179

Wang Delin, the nine-year-old beloved son of Wang Gaosun, a Ningbo architect residing at No. 2 Dafeng Lane, Huanlong Road in the French Concession, was suddenly kidnapped by bandits who broke into his home at 5:00 AM on December 28th of last year. They hid him away and demanded a huge ransom for his release. Negotiations failed, and it wasn't until April of this year that the case was solved by the Public Concession Police. The hostage was rescued from No. 511 in the Lüehong'an Lane, Laobazi (Old Race Course). Subsequently, the kidnappers Wang Yuanwei, Zhang Xiaomao, Yao Sheng, Xiang Ma Shi, Shi Yu Shi, Xi Ma Shi, Qian Ziming, Li Xilin, Chen Guoqian, Wu Yesong, Qian Changmei, Chen Abing, Chen Qiu Shi, Chen Zhang Shi, Zhang Wang Shi, Chen Zhang Shi, Wu Xiangfeng, Shen Qian Shi, and others (mostly from Shaoxing) – eighteen men and women in total – were apprehended. Because it was discovered that they had also committed a kidnapping case in the Public Concession, they were first sent to the First Special District Court for trial. (Wang was sentenced to life imprisonment, Zhang Xiaomao to ten and a half years, and Yao Sheng to nine and a half years.) On the 22nd of last month, Inspector Jin Jiulin of the Special Agency of the French Police, along with detectives, went to the First Special Court to transfer Wang and the other criminals to the French Police Station. The following morning, they were sent to the Third Special District Court for interrogation and investigation. Later, it was found that twelve of the men and women from Qian Ziming downwards were not involved in the case. No public prosecution was initiated, and the court was asked to rule for their release and return them to the First Special Court for disposal. The police investigation of Wang Yuanwei and the other six male and female criminals has now concluded. Yesterday afternoon, they were sent back to the court for questioning. (The fourth defendant, Xiang Ma Shi, was not sent to court because she was in the final month of her pregnancy and was sent to Guangci Hospital for childbirth.) Judge Li Changnian, accompanied by clerk Wang Baoxun, ascended to the Criminal Court No. 1 for interrogation. First, the police lawyer Gu Shouxi presented the case and the police investigation process. He stated that the case was initiated by Zhang Genfu, who is still at large. He ordered Wang Yuanwei to gather a gang to carry out the plan and discussed it with Ying Weishui, who is also at large, who agreed to be responsible for all expenses. After the agreement, Wang gathered the second and third defendants to carry out the plan together. In advance, they obtained two pistols from the hall for backup and rented No. 1 Xinyi Lane, Xujiahui Road, as the place to hide the hostage. On the morning of December 28th at 5:00 AM, Wang gave one of the pistols to the second defendant, Zhang Xiaomao, and ordered him and the third defendant, Yao Sheng, to wait at the entrance of Dafeng Lane, Huanlong Road. He then rented a car from the Zhongxi Motor Company on Caishi Road. He rode to the intersection of Jin Shenfu Road and Gao Naiyi Road, told the car to stop, got out and went to Dafeng Lane, Huanlong Road, to meet Zhang and Yao. The two men then held guns and broke into the plaintiff's house. Wang and Zhang scared away the family members of the house owner, and Yao Sheng immediately took the child Wang Delin, who was lying in bed, and carried him out. They hired a rickshaw to the intersection of Jin Shenfu Road and Gao Naiyi Road, got into the car, and sent him to No. 1 Xinyi Lane, Xujiahui Road, to hide him. They notified Ying Weishui and sent a letter to the plaintiff demanding a huge ransom for his release. On February 2nd of this year, on Ying's instructions, they moved the hostage to No. 511 Hong'an Lane, Laobazi, and recruited the two female bandits, Xiang Ma Shi and Shen Ma Shi, to guard him. After the case was discovered, the defendants were arrested. They all confessed to the above facts. The police are now prosecuting them in accordance with Article 1, Paragraph 1 of the Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits and are requesting that they be interrogated and dealt with according to the law. The fifth defendant, Shi Yu Shi, claimed that she was going to visit the sixth defendant, Shen Ma Shi, when she was arrested and that she was not involved in the case. She requested that the court investigate. The court verified the report and ordered the defendants to be taken down and questioned one by one separately. The defendants all confessed that they had carried out the kidnapping and guarded the hostage. They also said that Zhang Genfu, who is at large, initiated the plan and that Ying Weishui agreed to provide the funds. The court then summoned the kidnapped Wang Delin to the stand to question him about the kidnapping. After the questioning, the court announced that the case would be adjourned to the 20th and that a defense lawyer would be appointed to the case for further interrogation. The defendants were returned to the police station for detention.

Chen You Ting Commits Suicide Due To Despair After His Wife's Death And Loss Of Employment 180

Chen You Ting, a native of Wenzhou, was 27 years old. He used to work as a waiter for a Westerner. A month ago, his wife suddenly became critically ill in his hometown. Because of this, Chen resigned from his job and returned home to visit her. Unexpectedly, when he arrived home, his wife had already passed away. After hearing the news, Chen was extremely grief-stricken. He had no choice but to take care of the funeral arrangements. Later, he returned to Shanghai and stayed with his brother, Chen Youxiu, at No. 1054 Yuyuan Road. Recently, Chen repeatedly asked his friends to help him find a suitable job, but he was unable to find one. As a result, he lost both his money and his wife, and he felt increasingly frustrated. The day before yesterday, he suddenly had the idea of ending his life. He went out alone and bought opium, which he secretly swallowed. Later, his brother noticed and sent him to the Red Cross Hospital for treatment. However, the treatment was ineffective, and he soon died. The hospital reported to the Jing'an Temple Police Station, which ordered Detective Shi Huanting to investigate. The body was then taken to the Philan Road morgue. Yesterday morning, Zhang Junqing, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, arrived at the morgue to examine the body. He then ascended to the court and questioned Chen Youxiu, the brother of the deceased, who stated that his brother had recently used up all his money because his wife had suddenly died. In addition, he was currently unemployed. As a result, he committed suicide out of resentment. After hearing the statement, Zhang Jun ruled that the deceased, Chen You Ting, had indeed died from opium poisoning. The body was handed over to his brother, Chen Youxiu, who signed a guarantee to take it back for burial.

| The Reason For Suicide Remains Unclear |

The Italian Consulate at No. 555 Jing'an Temple Road in the Public Concession has recently been renovated and looks brand new. At night, a worker is assigned by the foreman to guard the building. It wasn't until yesterday morning that the people in the consulate discovered the body. The local security officer has already requested an autopsy from the court.

Pan Zhao Shi, a native of Ningbo, was 31 years old. She lived in the Dingxing Printing Factory at No. 326 Pingwang Street, Wuma Road. Zhu Chengqing Stabs Himself in the Throat 186

| Throat Not Severed, Possible to Save |

Zhu Chengqing, a native of Pinghu, was 50 years old. He was a silk inspector in the silk department of the Zhengda Silk Factory on Tiantong Road, Zhabei. He was trusted by the manager of the factory, Cha Jianshi, and others. At the same time, Zhu was also very diligent in his work. Although he occasionally had minor illnesses, he never asked for leave to rest. Therefore, recently, Zhu became weak and ill. Manager Cha Jianshi repeatedly told him to ask for leave to recuperate, but he never did. Recently, the manager and colleagues of the factory, seeing that Zhu was getting weaker and weaker, repeatedly advised him to rest. Zhu finally asked for leave the day before yesterday, but because he did not want to leave the factory, he still stayed in the factory. Unexpectedly, at around 2:00 AM yesterday morning, Zhu suddenly used a small paper cutter to stab a hole in his throat. Immediately, blood gushed out, and he fell to the ground in extreme pain. A colleague in the bedroom suddenly heard Zhu moaning and got up to check. He saw Zhu lying in a pool of blood, still bleeding from his throat. When asked why, he was vague and ambiguous. The colleague changed his bloody clothes and rushed him to Tongren Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, his blood vessels were not injured, and there was no major problem. He is still hospitalized for treatment. At the same time, the factory urgently telegraphed Zhu's family to call his wife to Shanghai. As for why he suddenly had the idea of ending his life, the people in the factory said that Zhu had suffered a huge loss in the silk cocoon business, and perhaps this was the reason.

Conviction for Secretly Manufacturing Red Pills in Ningbo 187

West Detective Hua Men of the Putuo Road Police Station, Chief Detective Feng Baishun, Detective Chen Hongbin, and others cracked a secret organization manufacturing red pills at No. 8 Wuding Road and No. 32 Wuding Lane on the 24th of last month. They arrested Liu Lianchang, Yang Baosheng, Zhou Laisheng, and a woman, Pan Shen Shi, all from Zhejiang, and seized a large number of red pills and machines. They were sent to the First Special District Court, where they were repeatedly interrogated. The trial has now concluded. Yesterday morning was the scheduled date for sentencing. The defendants' lawyers, Wu Linkun and Wang Shuxun, and the police lawyer, Zhang Shizhu, were all present in court to await the verdict. Judge Liu Yugui presided over the court and announced the verdict. Yang Baosheng was sentenced to one year of imprisonment, Liu Lianchang was fined 500 yuan, and Zhou Laisheng and Pan Shen Shi were found not guilty. All the seized items were confiscated according to the list. After hearing the verdict, the police lawyer Zhang immediately stated that he would appeal the cases of Liu and Zhou and requested that they be returned to custody during the appeal period. As for Pan Shen Shi, he abandoned the appeal. Liu's lawyer, Wang Shuxun, requested bail. Judge Liu then ordered that Liu Lianchang be allowed to post bail of 500 yuan and a guarantor who could be summoned at any time during the appeal. Zhou Laisheng was returned to custody, and Pan Shen Shi was released.

Adulterer Slashed Eleven Times 188

| Possible Risk to His Life |

Zhang Afu, a 60-year-old resident of Jiangbo Village, District 41, Luodian, Baoshan County, had a son named A Hong, 26 years old, and a daughter-in-law named Jin Shi, 25 years old. In December of last year, Jin Shi was seduced by Jiang Aju (23 years old), a nearby resident, and committed adultery in secret more than once. Recently, A Hong found out and secretly paid attention. At around 8:00 PM the night before last, Jiang Aju came again to try to be with Jin Shi. Zhang Afu and his son chased him out with kitchen knives. Jiang Aju was unable to escape and was slashed, fell to the ground, and bled profusely. The Public Security Bureau heard the alarm and arrested Zhang Afu and his son and Jin Shi and sent them to the Baoshan County Government for interrogation. The injured Jiang Aju was immediately taken to the hospital for treatment. He suffered three stab wounds to his right leg, two to his left leg, three to his left hand, one to his buttocks, and one to each of his left and right feet. His injuries were quite dangerous, and there was a possible risk to his life. However, according to the injured Jiang Aju, the incident was caused by a quarrel over money, and he did not admit to any adulterous behavior.

Six Letters of Extortion and One Bullet 189

| The Criminals Sentenced Separately |

Zhou A Si and Wu A Da, natives of Tongzhou, colluded with Zhang Huilin, who is at large, from May to June. They repeatedly wrote letters of extortion and delivered them to No. 287 Zhaofeng Road, demanding 1,000 yuan from Sun Yuanyou, a native of Nanjing. There were as many as six letters. Each letter contained one bullet and was written in strong language, threatening to take action if the money was not paid. The Huishan Police Station was informed and sent Detective Wang Jinsheng to arrest Zhou and Wu. They confessed that the rickshaw puller of the victim's family, Zhang Cai Gen, also known as A Er, was the informant. The detectives rushed to arrest Zhang and brought him to the police station. It was learned that Wu A Da wrote the extortion letters alone, but Wu denied it. The police asked him to write a confession in person for handwriting comparison. They were sent to the First Court. Zhou A Si admitted that he was fooled by Zhang Huilin, who is at large. Zhang Cai Gen's confession was evasive. Zhou A Si firmly denied that he wrote the extortion letters. The court ordered a detailed investigation and asked experts to study the handwriting on file. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zehan opened the court for further interrogation. The police lawyer Zhang Tianyin recounted the previous events and stated that the investigation revealed that Zhang Cai Gen had told Zhang Huilin, who is at large, that the Sun family was rich and that the younger master (Sun Yuanyou) was very timid after the death of the old master and that he could be intimidated with a letter of extortion and that there was hope. The victim was asked to come to court for questioning. According to Sun Yuanyou, after receiving the letter, the rickshaw puller Zhang Cai Gen said that he would not go to manage it because it was too dangerous. The three defendants were questioned, and their statements were the same as before, evading responsibility. The court declared that the letters written by Wu A Da and his confession written at the police station had been examined by the court's special appraiser, Mr. Yin. The six letters of extortion were entirely written by him without any doubt. Therefore, Zhou A Si was sentenced to five years of imprisonment, Wu A Da to three years of imprisonment, and Zhang Cai Gen to two years of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the final judgment were deducted from the sentence at the rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. The letters of extortion and bullets were confiscated.

▲Famous Suzhou Doctor Ni Xi Lai Shen for Consultation Doctor Ni is a disciple of Bao Biaofen, a well-known scholar in Wumen. ▲The Gospel of Hemoptysis Patients Doctor Zhang Ruwei of Daqing Lane, Nanjing Road, is skilled in treating internal medicine, gynecology, and otolaryngology. He has particularly rich experience in treating hemoptysis and pulmonary tuberculosis. The day before yesterday, a Mr. Yin on Shanhai Pass Road coughed up a basin of blood, which had not stopped for several days. Both Chinese and Western doctors were unable to do anything. After Mr. Zhang's prescription, the bleeding stopped immediately. After half a month of treatment, he recovered his health. Mr. Zhang said that from the end of spring to the beginning of summer this year, it was rainy and cold, and recently the weather has been sultry, with both dampness and heat accumulating, which makes blood vessels prone to rupture and rise. If the root cause is not treated, it will often be ineffective. It is heard that many patients with hemoptysis and pulmonary tuberculosis have been cured recently. Lawyer Wang Youlin of May Bellek Road believes in him very much and has hired him as a family medical consultant.

▲Zhuanqiao Free Medical Clinic to Open Tomorrow The Zhuanqiao Free Medical Clinic in Shanghai County was initiated by local people. It has been in preparation for two months. Now everything is ready, and it is scheduled to officially open tomorrow (15th) and will continue until August 13th. Whether it will continue depends on the amount of funding. The doctors hired by the clinic, including Qin Bowei, are all well-known experts in Pudong. This time, they are all participating on a voluntary basis, so the clinic will definitely benefit the community in a non-superficial way.

Letters to the Editor 197

To the Esteemed Editors,

Regarding the article "Zhabei Silk Factory Strikes Again Yesterday" in your newspaper's local section on July 13th, which stated, "…for Sunday overtime, according to regulations, each person should receive $0.58, but the factory only paid $0.50. Therefore, the workers questioned the factory. However, according to the factory's reply, the $0.08 was deducted at the request of the union to be handed over to the union…" this is far from the truth. An agreement was reached through mediation by the Social Affairs Bureau that overtime pay would be set at two working days per month, with wages at $0.50 per day, and Sunday overtime at $0.20 per week. This was published in your newspaper. Thus, since there was no $0.58 overtime pay, how could the union request the factory to deduct $0.08? The aforementioned news is clearly a misunderstanding and does not conform to the facts. We are deeply concerned that this may mislead the public and request an immediate correction.

Sincerely,

Shanghai Sixth District Raw Silk Industry Union
