Film Special

"Mmmmmmm"? 270

— Yin Xi

This is a new term from Hollywood

The new trend for modern women

Film fans, do you know? Hollywood has invented another new word! This word is "Mmmmmmm". How should this word be explained? If you string together seven (or a few more, it doesn't matter) M's, you can understand it. I am now translating this word as "唔丨丨丨". This "唔" is pronounced with an N sound. Although the sounds of M and N are quite different, one with closed lips and the other with open lips, when you see a woman's body and feel admiration that cannot be expressed in words, foreigners

say "Mmmmmmm" and Chinese people say "Nnnnnnnn". This is a very natural exclamation. Now I'm translating it as "唔丨丨丨", which should not be too far off.

What exactly is this "唔丨丨丨"? Some say it's a variation of "It". "It" with a little more flesh becomes "Mmmmmmm". Originally, Clara Bow was a muscular and plump "It girl", but now that she has returned from Europe, her waist has gained another inch, and she has become a modern Mmmmmmm girl. There is also a Miss Mae West, who is now a sexy (M Ses appeal) star. Of course, she has a firm grasp of this modern Mmmmmmm. So we can say that the fashion of women's bodies, since a busybody found "It" in Clara Bow, later there was an even more busy person, who generalized it, transformed it into S.A., so that ordinary women, anyone can have it (not only women, men can also have S.A.); anyone can train it, if they lack it. Now it's good, I don't know which busybody, fearing that the world is at peace, strongly emphasized a kind of S.A. and gave it a new name, called "Mmmmmmm".

The fashion of women's bodies, of course, also has a sense of the times. So a few years ago, when slim waists were emphasized, many stars were afraid of gaining weight. Greta Nissen starved herself for eighteen days to make her body thinner. Now that Mmmmmmm has emerged, women are again emphasizing "abundance with surplus, softness as if boneless". So Greta Nissen, who used to starve herself to slim her waist, is now preparing a lot of sweets, eating them at any time, to make her body grow fatter day by day.

Some say then isn't "Mmmmmmm" just healthy beauty? No. Healthy beauty lies in firm muscles and sufficient blood, while "Mmmmmmm" is something else. It has a moving sex appeal on top of health. Of course, these are two very difficult things to separate, but clever people can easily understand their differences. If we add some sexual temptation to healthy beauty, then it becomes "唔".

But after talking for so long, the author is just telling readers about some new Hollywood trends, and is not advising Chinese actresses to eat more meat, more sweets, and sleep more to make their bodies fatter. To be honest, Mae West is the only fat woman with curves and sex appeal in Hollywood. Moreover, although Mae West's body is fat, she exercises her body every day to prevent her weight from increasing further. Many women see that Mae West is interestingly fat and also want to gain weight, but they may not get the benefits of being fat, but instead become bloated and inconvenient to move.

Film Reviews

Review of "The Night Mayor" The Night Mayor 271

— Ling He

Recently, film titles have suddenly become popular with direct translations, such as "Eagle Song" and "White Sisters"...and the "Night Mayor" showing at Cathay is also like this. As for whether this is a good phenomenon, it is not discussed in this article, but it is just mentioned in passing.

Hollywood producers are very obviously showing a panic about subject matter. This is something we can observe with a little attention. However, it's definitely not that there are no real subjects, but rather that they are unwilling to find a way out in real social events. So they are most happy to spend money and time on empty stories, directly allowing idle audiences to get empty entertainment in a few hours.

The fictional nature of the story of "The Night Mayor" should be the feeling of every audience member who has seen this film. Since this is the case, we should not pursue its authenticity. However, I always feel that such a story is rather boring.

If someone says that the intention of this film is mainly to satirize certain chaotic bureaucrats, of course, we can see this intention from the beginning of the film to the mayor's clandestine rendezvous with a dancer at a hotel, but in the end, this mayor has to become a virtuous gentleman, so he actually rationally officiates at the wedding for his rival in love, and even at the end leads the citizens in a demonstration parade with the "We Want Beer" sign, naturally indicating support for Roosevelt's policies. As for the dancer being willing to sacrifice the position of the mayor's wife to marry a journalist, saying it's for the mayor's political future, that's even more wonderful. So this is definitely not satirizing the political authorities, but rather the painstaking effort of a slave advising his master. However, the power of this kind of preaching is obviously very weak.

In terms of performance, some may consider that the bright and frivolous style is relatively novel. Regarding this point, we certainly cannot ignore that this style is quite suitable for the plot, but the deliberately exaggerated tension in some scenes inevitably makes people suspect the destruction of the uniformity that every film should have. Lee Tracy's movements are certainly brisk, but some occasions doubly reveal frivolity. As for whether the dignified officials of the United States are so dissolute and unrestrained, it is difficult for us Chinese to understand.

However, the director's petty bourgeois grievances are more or less expressed in this work. His criticism of officials in the first half is indeed a painstaking depiction. The mayor sleeps late and doesn't answer the phone, the mayor's governance is only for unveiling statues, throwing balls for the stadium, giving speeches for boxing matches, and finally officiating at the wedding for his lover, and hooking up with young girls in dance classes. As for putting a rival in love in jail for a woman, sometimes indulging, sometimes arresting, doing whatever one wants, and also saying that the mayor's secretary actually killed someone innocently, this kind of description is truly extremely vicious. At this point, the Chinese audience looks back, I wonder what their feelings are.

Fox Company's great production "Warrior's Husband" starring Elissa Landi, the female lead of "Roman Scandals", is the first major production by Jesse L. Lasky, the former Paramount production tycoon, after joining "Fox". The costumes in the whole film are antique, extremely gorgeous, and are showing in "Nanjing".

Rasputin 272

— Mi Wu

丨Showing at the Shanghai Grand Theater丨

Who says White Russians have no motherland to protect them? Their motherland is the capitalist countries of the world. This time, two Rasputins, it is said that the censorship result showed no "insult to the Russian Emperor", but finally, due to the opposition of the White Russians, only one German-produced version was publicly screened in the Shanghai Grand Theater in the Chinese concession.

The story is a Russian legend, so there is no need to repeat it here. But in this story, there are many things revealed to us.

We know that the transition from the era of theocracy to the era of monarchy (this is naturally not the stage theorist's, that kind of mechanical lawlessness, at the same time, theocracy and monarchy are sometimes mutually combined.) went through a struggle. Rasputin is a representative of the supernatural, and although the Emperor and Empress are respected as the mother of the nation, they deeply believe in and respect him because their beloved son was treated by him. This shows how much the older generation respects theocracy, which also shows that the monarchy cannot but bow before theocracy. But the younger generation is not like this, he wants to resist, he wants to overthrow this so-called divine power, although the Russian Crown Prince's own illness was cured by Rasputin, he painstakingly planned to murder him, and finally, after the poison cake was ineffective, he followed up with five bullets and killed Rasputin. Doesn't this clearly show that the monarchy has triumphed over theocracy?

Secondly, this film is made with an antagonistic attitude towards "God" (Rasputin). Therefore, not only does it finally show Rasputin's death, but it also exposes Rasputin's debauchery thoroughly. Even his meeting with his old lover, Rosa, is met with a painful beating by her father, resulting in injury on the road.

I don't know how other audiences, or critics, understand this Rasputin. But I always think that the central consciousness of Rasputin cannot be grasped unless it is explained in this way. Because this is not only the consciousness of the film, it is also the consciousness of this legend.

As for technique, the style of German films has always been different from that of Hollywood. It does not have the modernity of Hollywood, so they are very happy to show films about ancient stories. "Dragon Soaring Phoenix Dancing" is like this! "White Demon" is like this; this "Rasputin" is a work in the same style as the aforementioned films. It often has very long shots, expressing a certain point extremely freely: unlike the fast changes of shots in American films, which make people dizzying. As for the use of sound, it is another special feature of Germany. The director tries to pay attention to the coordination of sound and shadow, so that the audience can get the enjoyment of the ears and eyes. The actors naturally have Conrad Veidt as the best. He is very reliable, and also very profoundly expresses the actions and even emotions that the character in the play should have. The others are also competent.

The Secret of the American Garbo 273

— Shi Chun

Kathleen Hepburn, known as the American Garbo, although she has only starred in two films in Hollywood, one "A Bill of Divorcement" and one "A Great Desire", her reputation has surpassed that of general veteran stars in Hollywood.

Since Kathleen has attracted the attention of the masses, many journalists have spent a lot of time asking Kathleen about her background, family situation, and how she entered the art world. However, the American Garbo not only looks like the Swedish Garbo, but also has a similar personality. She is very secretive and keeps her mouth shut about issues such as family situation and background, and never reveals the truth to others. As a result, rumors abound. Some said that Kathleen had several children who were all at home, others said that she had already been married but had no children. Some said that she had a degree from Bryn Mawr College, while others said that she had never been to college. Some even said that she had sixteen million in property, but others said that she had no property and only lived on her salary. Discussions are endless, and it is not known whose words are true.

Later, someone finally found out everything about her. It turned out that Kathleen was from Hartford in the eastern United States. Her father was Dr. Soames Hepburn, who was highly respected, but had no property. She had a total of six siblings, one of whom died, and there are now five. She is the third. She did go to college, studying drama, but did not graduate. She has been married for three years and her husband is a businessman, but she has never had children.

Kathleen's secret has finally been revealed to everyone. Here we can also admire Hollywood's volunteer detectives.

The Film Novel Adorable (9) 274

— Si Ying

Karel Konradt took the princess's letter and ran to the prime minister's office to submit the letter to the prime minister. The prime minister opened the letter and read it, feeling ecstatic. It turned out that the princess had agreed to the marriage with Prince Bondenvedulo. The Prime Minister said to Karel, "Congratulations, congratulations, General!" He then ordered Prince Bondenvedulo to set off quickly. The palace also prepared to hold a dance party to welcome Prince Bondenvedulo. The princess regretted it at this time, but it was too late, because the prime minister threatened that if this marriage was stopped halfway, it would definitely cause a war between the two countries.

The day of the dance party arrived. In the vast and gorgeous dance hall, the prime minister led the princess in, surrounded by the wives and children of the ministers, dressed in colorful clothes. After a while, the guards blew their horns, announcing that Prince Bondenvedulo had arrived. The prince was a young invalid, with a dull look, like a zombie crawling out of a grave. The princess seemed very disdainful, raising her head even higher, and reluctantly stretched out her hand to let Prince Bondenvedulo kiss it. The music started, playing the waltz that the princess and Karel had played when they first met that night. The princess said angrily to the prince, "Let's dance." She really couldn't bear it anymore, because Karel stood beside her, staring at the princess with fierce eyes, making her feel ashamed. But the prince didn't dance. When he saw Karel standing beside him, he greeted him and said, "Please represent me, I can't dance, is that okay?"

"Is that okay?" Before Karel could finish speaking, he immediately put his arms around the princess, and without waiting for the princess to agree, he started dancing. The prime minister saw that things were not good and immediately stopped him, but Karel and the princess had already squeezed past the crowd. The prime minister squeezed in and out of the crowd, looking for Karel and the princess. At this time, the Emperor arrived, but the prime minister did not know and was still looking for the princess and Karel. When someone pulled him and told him that the Emperor had arrived, the Emperor had already entered. The princess hurriedly went up to greet him, she must see the Emperor this time. The Emperor saw the princess. He asked her, "This sister of yours is so good, she doesn't even come to see me after returning from school. The princess took the Emperor's little hand and comforted him, "Good brother, I have wanted to see you many times, but the prime minister has always stopped me and wouldn't let me see you." The Emperor said angrily to the prime minister: "Good prime minister, I don't need you anymore, you go home!" The Emperor saw that his sister was so beautiful and asked her why no one wanted to marry her? The princess pointed to Prince Bondenvedulo and said, "He wants to marry me." Prince Bondenvedulo felt a little ashamed, and he said to the Emperor, "Our marriage cannot succeed. My heart is already focused on our lovely mummy." The Emperor laughed and said, "Great, you go back and find your mummy!"

The princess put her hands on the Emperor's shoulders and whispered a few words in the Emperor's ear. The Emperor turned around, patted Karel's shoulder, and said to the princess, "How about this person? Are you willing to marry him? I think he should be made a prince."

The princess quickly replied, "Good, good, you should make him a prince." (The End)
